# RunAtlas Environment Variables

# ========================================
# Current Mode: JSON Files (works out of box)
# ========================================
# No external services required — all data is self-contained in JSON files.
# Just run: npm install && npm run dev

# ========================================
# Future Mode: PostgreSQL + Prisma
# ========================================
# DATABASE_URL=postgresql://user:password@localhost:5432/runatlas
#
# Setup:
# 1. Install PostgreSQL
# 2. Create database: createdb runatlas
# 3. Set DATABASE_URL above
# 4. Run: npx prisma db push
# 5. Seed: npx ts-node prisma/seed.ts

# Optional: Custom port
# PORT=3000

# Optional: Analytics
# NEXT_PUBLIC_POSTHOG_KEY=phc_xxxxx
# NEXT_PUBLIC_POSTHOG_HOST=https://app.posthog.com

# RunAtlas V4 — AI Capability Engine

> Not just a directory. A problem-solving platform for the AI ecosystem.

## 🚀 What's New in V4

### Core Architecture
- **503 AI Tools** with enriched metadata (API, OSS, platforms, capabilities)
- **16 Capabilities** (Text Gen, Image Gen, Video, Voice, Code, etc.)
- **20 Use Cases** with full pipeline workflows
- **10 Workflows** with step-by-step tool connections
- **Prisma + PostgreSQL** schema with seed script for database migration
- **Smart Search** with semantic capability mapping

### New Pages
| Page | Route | Description |
|------|-------|-------------|
| 🧠 Capability Map | `/capabilities` | Tools organized by AI capabilities |
| 🧰 Stack Builder | `/stack-builder` | Build your personal AI tool stack |
| ⏳ Timeline | `/timeline` | AI tool history 2020–2025 |
| 🔥 Trending | `/trending` | Hot tools, top rated, category breakdown |
| 📋 Use Cases | `/use-cases` | Problem → Solution → Tools |
| 🔗 Workflows | `/workflows` | AI pipeline visualization |
| ⚡ Compare | `/compare` | Side-by-side tool comparison |
| 🌍 Globe | `/globe` | Global AI company map |
| 🔗 Knowledge Graph | `/graph` | AI ecosystem relationships |
| 🏢 Companies | `/companies` | AI company directory |
| 📝 Submit Tool | `/submit-tool` | Community tool submissions |
| 🔍 Search | `/search` | Smart AI-powered search |
| 🛡️ Admin | `/admin/submissions` | Submission moderation dashboard |

### SEO Landing Pages
10 optimized pages at `/best/[slug]`:
- `/best/ai-tools-for-writing`
- `/best/free-ai-tools`
- `/best/ai-tools-for-youtube`
- `/best/ai-tools-for-marketing`
- `/best/ai-coding-tools`
- `/best/ai-image-generators`
- `/best/ai-video-tools`
- `/best/ai-tools-for-students`
- `/best/open-source-ai-tools`
- `/best/ai-voice-tools`

### Import Pipeline
```
scripts/scraper.ts     → Discover tools (GitHub, Product Hunt, Directories)
scripts/import-tools.ts → Import & deduplicate into database
scripts/normalize.ts    → Data quality & normalization
```

## 📦 Setup

```bash
# Install dependencies
npm install

# Set up environment
cp .env.example .env
# Edit .env with your database URL

# Run with JSON (default — no database needed)
npm run dev

# OR: Set up PostgreSQL
npx prisma migrate dev
npx ts-node prisma/seed.ts
```

## 🔑 Key Concepts

### AI Capability Engine
Users search by **problem**, not by tool name:
```
"I want to create YouTube videos" →
  Script: ChatGPT
  Thumbnail: Midjourney
  Video: Runway
  Voice: ElevenLabs
```

### Capability Graph
Tools connect to capabilities, not just categories:
```
ChatGPT → Text Generation + Chatbot + Code Generation
Runway → Video Generation + Image Editing
```

### Smart Search
Semantic search maps natural language to capabilities:
```
"remove background from image" → Image Editing tools
"automate my marketing" → Marketing + Automation tools
```

## 🛠 Tech Stack
- **Next.js 14** with App Router + ISR
- **TypeScript** throughout
- **Tailwind CSS** with dark theme
- **Prisma** for database (optional — works with JSON too)
- **Three.js / Globe.gl** for globe visualization
- **D3 / Force Graph** for knowledge graph

## 📈 SEO Strategy
- ISR with `revalidate = 86400` for all pages
- Dynamic sitemap with 500+ URLs
- Structured metadata on every page
- SEO landing pages targeting high-volume keywords
- robots.txt configured

Built with ❤️ by RunAtlas

║ FILE: ./app/admin/submissions/page.tsx
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

import { getSubmissions } from "@/lib/db"

export const dynamic = "force-dynamic"

export default function AdminSubmissionsPage() {
  const submissions = getSubmissions()
  const pending = submissions.filter((s) => s.status === "pending")
  const approved = submissions.filter((s) => s.status === "approved")
  const rejected = submissions.filter((s) => s.status === "rejected")

  const STATUS_STYLE: Record<string, string> = {
    pending: "bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400 border-yellow-500/30",
    approved: "bg-green-500/20 text-green-400 border-green-500/30",
    rejected: "bg-red-500/20 text-red-400 border-red-500/30",
  }

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-[#0a0a0f] text-white px-6 py-12">
      <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto">
        <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-8">🛡️ Admin — Tool Submissions</h1>

        {/* Stats */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-10">
          {[
            { label: "Pending Review", count: pending.length, color: "text-yellow-400" },
            { label: "Approved", count: approved.length, color: "text-green-400" },
            { label: "Rejected", count: rejected.length, color: "text-red-400" },
          ].map((stat) => (
            <div key={stat.label} className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl p-5 text-center">
              <div className={`text-3xl font-bold mb-1 ${stat.color}`}>{stat.count}</div>
              <div className="text-gray-400 text-sm">{stat.label}</div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Submissions table */}
        <div className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl overflow-hidden">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="w-full">
              <thead>
                <tr className="border-b border-white/10">
                  <th className="text-left p-4 text-gray-400 text-sm">Tool Name</th>
                  <th className="text-left p-4 text-gray-400 text-sm">Category</th>
                  <th className="text-left p-4 text-gray-400 text-sm">Website</th>
                  <th className="text-left p-4 text-gray-400 text-sm">Status</th>
                  <th className="text-left p-4 text-gray-400 text-sm">Submitted</th>
                  <th className="text-left p-4 text-gray-400 text-sm">Actions</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody>
                {submissions.length === 0 ? (
                  <tr>
                    <td colSpan={6} className="text-center p-8 text-gray-500">No submissions yet</td>
                  </tr>
                ) : (
                  submissions.map((sub) => (
                    <tr key={sub.id} className="border-b border-white/5 hover:bg-white/5">
                      <td className="p-4 font-medium text-white">{sub.name}</td>
                      <td className="p-4 text-gray-400 text-sm">{sub.category}</td>
                      <td className="p-4">
                        <a href={sub.website} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" className="text-indigo-400 hover:underline text-sm truncate block max-w-[200px]">
                          {sub.website}
                        </a>
                      </td>
                      <td className="p-4">
                        <span className={`text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded-full border ${STATUS_STYLE[sub.status]}`}>
                          {sub.status}
                        </span>
                      </td>
                      <td className="p-4 text-gray-500 text-xs">
                        {new Date(sub.created_at).toLocaleDateString()}
                      </td>
                      <td className="p-4">
                        {sub.status === "pending" && (
                          <div className="flex gap-2">
                            <form action={`/api/admin/submissions/${sub.id}/approve`} method="POST">
                              <button className="text-xs bg-green-500/20 text-green-400 border border-green-500/30 px-3 py-1 rounded-lg hover:bg-green-500/30 transition-colors">
                                Approve
                              </button>
                            </form>
                            <form action={`/api/admin/submissions/${sub.id}/reject`} method="POST">
                              <button className="text-xs bg-red-500/20 text-red-400 border border-red-500/30 px-3 py-1 rounded-lg hover:bg-red-500/30 transition-colors">
                                Reject
                              </button>
                            </form>
                          </div>
                        )}
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                  ))
                )}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </main>
  )
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/api/admin/submissions/[id]/approve/route.ts
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

import { updateSubmissionStatus } from "@/lib/db"
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"

export async function POST(
  req: NextRequest,
  { params }: { params: { id: string } }
) {
  try {
    updateSubmissionStatus(params.id, "approved")
    return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/admin/submissions", req.url))
  } catch (e) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "Failed to approve" }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/api/companies/[slug]/route.ts
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server";
import { getCompanyBySlug, getCompanyTools } from "@/atlas/companies";

export async function GET(
  request: NextRequest,
  { params }: { params: Promise<{ slug: string }> }
) {
  const { slug } = await params;
  const company = getCompanyBySlug(slug);

  if (!company) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "Company not found" }, { status: 404 });
  }

  const tools = getCompanyTools(slug);
  return NextResponse.json({ ...company, toolDetails: tools });
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/api/companies/route.ts

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server";
import { getTopCompanies, getAllCompanies } from "@/atlas/companies";

export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {
  const { searchParams } = new URL(request.url);
  const limit = parseInt(searchParams.get("limit") || "50");
  const companies = getTopCompanies(limit);
  return NextResponse.json({ companies, total: getAllCompanies().length });
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/api/compare/route.ts
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server";
import { getToolsForComparison } from "@/atlas/compare";

export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {
  const { searchParams } = new URL(request.url);
  const slugsParam = searchParams.get("slugs") || "";

  if (!slugsParam.trim()) {
    return NextResponse.json([]);
  }

  const slugs = slugsParam.split(",").filter(Boolean);

  if (slugs.length > 4) {
    return NextResponse.json(
      { error: "Maximum 4 tools can be compared at once" },
      { status: 400 }
    );
  }

  const tools = await getToolsForComparison(slugs);
  return NextResponse.json(tools);
}

╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/api/search/route.ts

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server";
import { searchTools } from "@/atlas/search";

export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {
  const { searchParams } = new URL(request.url);
  const q = searchParams.get("q") || "";

  if (!q.trim()) {
    return NextResponse.json([]);
  }

  const results = await searchTools(q);
  return NextResponse.json(results);
}

import { NextResponse } from "next/server";
import { getToolStats, getCategories } from "@/atlas/tools";
import { getCompaniesByCountry } from "@/atlas/companies";

export async function GET() {
  const stats = getToolStats();
  const categories = getCategories();
  const byCountry = getCompaniesByCountry();
  
  return NextResponse.json({
    ...stats,
    categories,
    companiesByCountry: byCountry,
  });
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/api/submit/route.ts
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

import { addSubmission, type Submission } from "@/lib/db"
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
import crypto from "crypto"

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await req.json()

    // Validate required fields
    if (!body.name || !body.website || !body.category || !body.description) {
      return NextResponse.json(
        { error: "Missing required fields: name, website, category, description" },
        { status: 400 }
      )
    }

    // Basic spam protection - check if website looks valid
    if (!body.website.startsWith("http")) {
      return NextResponse.json(
        { error: "Website must start with http:// or https://" },
        { status: 400 }
      )
    }

    const submission: Submission = {
      id: crypto.randomUUID(),
      name: String(body.name).slice(0, 100),
      website: String(body.website).slice(0, 500),
      category: String(body.category).slice(0, 50),
      description: String(body.description).slice(0, 1000),
      pricing: body.pricing ? String(body.pricing).slice(0, 50) : undefined,
      email: body.email ? String(body.email).slice(0, 200) : undefined,
      status: "pending",
      created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    }

    addSubmission(submission)

    return NextResponse.json({
      success: true,
      message: "Tool submitted successfully! It will be reviewed within 24-48 hours.",
      id: submission.id,
    })
  } catch (e) {
    console.error("Submit error:", e)
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "Internal server error" }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

║ FILE: ./app/best/[slug]/page.tsx
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

import { getTools } from "@/lib/db"
import { notFound } from "next/navigation"
import Link from "next/link"
import type { Metadata } from "next"

export const revalidate = 86400

// Map SEO slugs to query configs
const SEO_PAGES: Record<string, {
  title: string
  description: string
  category?: string
  tags?: string[]
  pricing?: string
  heading: string
  subheading: string
}> = {
  "ai-tools-for-writing": {
    title: "Best AI Writing Tools 2025 | RunAtlas",
    description: "Discover the top AI writing tools for content creation, copywriting, and SEO. Compare features, pricing, and reviews.",

export async function generateStaticParams() {
  return Object.keys(SEO_PAGES).map((slug) => ({ slug }))
}

export async function generateMetadata({ params }: { params: { slug: string } }): Promise<Metadata> {
  const config = SEO_PAGES[params.slug]
  if (!config) return {}
  return {
    title: config.title,
    description: config.description,
    openGraph: {
      title: config.title,
      description: config.description,
    }
  }
}

export default function BestToolsPage({ params }: { params: { slug: string } }) {
  const config = SEO_PAGES[params.slug]
  if (!config) notFound()

  let tools = getTools()

  // Filter by config
  if (config.category) {
    tools = tools.filter((t) => t.category === config.category)
  }
  if (config.pricing === "free") {
    tools = tools.filter(
      (t) =>
        t.pricing.toLowerCase() === "free" ||
        t.pricing.toLowerCase() === "freemium" ||
        t.pricing_details?.free_tier === true
    )
  }
  if (config.pricing === "open_source") {
    tools = tools.filter(
      (t) =>
        t.pricing.toLowerCase() === "open_source" ||
        t.tags?.includes("open-source") ||
        t.tags?.includes("open_source")
    )
  }
  if (config.tags) {
    const tags = config.tags
    tools = tools.filter((t) =>
      tags.some((tag) =>
        t.tags?.some((tt) => tt.toLowerCase().includes(tag.toLowerCase())) ||
        t.category.toLowerCase().includes(tag.toLowerCase())
      )
    )
  }

  // Sort by rating
  tools = [...tools].sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating)

  const PRICING_COLOR: Record<string, string> = {
    free: "bg-green-500/20 text-green-400",
    freemium: "bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400",
    paid: "bg-orange-500/20 text-orange-400",
    open_source: "bg-purple-500/20 text-purple-400",
  }

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-[#0a0a0f] text-white">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-6 py-16">
        {/* Breadcrumb */}
        <nav className="text-sm text-gray-500 mb-8">
          <Link href="/" className="hover:text-white">Home</Link>
          {" / "}
          <span className="text-gray-300">{config.heading}</span>
        </nav>

        <div className="mb-12">
          <h1 className="text-4xl md:text-6xl font-bold mb-4 bg-gradient-to-r from-white to-gray-400 bg-clip-text text-transparent">
            {config.heading}
          </h1>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xl mb-6">{config.subheading}</p>
          <div className="text-gray-500 text-sm">
            {tools.length} tools found
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-5">
          {tools.map((tool, i) => (
            <Link
              key={tool.slug}
              href={`/tool/${tool.slug}`}
              className="group bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/10 hover:border-indigo-500/40 rounded-xl p-5 transition-all"
            >
              <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-3">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <span className="text-gray-500 text-sm font-bold">#{i + 1}</span>
                  <h2 className="font-bold text-white group-hover:text-indigo-400 transition-colors">
                    {tool.name}
                  </h2>
                </div>
                <span className={`text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded-full ${PRICING_COLOR[tool.pricing.toLowerCase()] ?? "bg-white/10 text-gray-400"}`}>
                  {tool.pricing}
                </span>
              </div>
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm mb-3 line-clamp-2">{tool.description}</p>
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
                  <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★</span>
                  <span className="text-sm text-gray-300">{tool.rating.toFixed(1)}</span>
                </div>
                {tool.company && (
                  <span className="text-xs text-gray-500">{tool.company}</span>
                )}
              </div>
            </Link>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* SEO footer content */}
        <div className="mt-16 prose prose-invert max-w-none">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white mb-4">About These Tools</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-400">
            RunAtlas has curated and reviewed the {config.heading.toLowerCase()} available today.
            Our database includes {tools.length}+ options with detailed reviews, pricing information,
            and user ratings to help you find the perfect tool for your needs.
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </main>
  )
}

import { getCapabilities, getTools, getWorkflows } from "@/lib/db"
import { notFound } from "next/navigation"
import Link from "next/link"
import type { Metadata } from "next"

export const revalidate = 86400

export async function generateStaticParams() {
  const capabilities = getCapabilities()
  return capabilities.map((c) => ({ slug: c.slug }))
}

export async function generateMetadata({
  params,
}: {
  params: { slug: string }
}): Promise<Metadata> {
  const cap = getCapabilities().find((c) => c.slug === params.slug)
  if (!cap) return {}
  return {
    title: `Best AI ${cap.name} Tools 2025 | RunAtlas`,
    description: `Discover the best AI tools for ${cap.name.toLowerCase()}. Compare features, pricing, and reviews of ${cap.description.toLowerCase()}.`,
  }
}

export default function CapabilityDetailPage({
  params,
}: {
  params: { slug: string }
}) {
  const capabilities = getCapabilities()
  const cap = capabilities.find((c) => c.slug === params.slug)
  if (!cap) notFound()

  const allTools = getTools()
  const tools = allTools
    .filter((t) => t.capabilities?.includes(cap.slug))
    .sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating)

  const workflows = getWorkflows().filter((w) =>
    w.steps.some((s) => {
      const tool = allTools.find((t) => t.slug === s.tool_slug)
      return tool?.capabilities?.includes(cap.slug)
    })
  )

  const freeTools = tools.filter(
    (t) => t.pricing === "free" || t.pricing === "freemium" || t.pricing_details?.free_tier
  )
  const apiTools = tools.filter((t) => t.has_api)
  const ossTools = tools.filter((t) => t.is_open_source)

  const PRICING_COLOR: Record<string, string> = {
    free: "bg-green-500/20 text-green-400",
    freemium: "bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400",
    paid: "bg-orange-500/20 text-orange-400",
    open_source: "bg-purple-500/20 text-purple-400",
  }

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-[#0a0a0f] text-white">
      <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-6 py-16">
        {/* Breadcrumb */}
        <nav className="text-sm text-gray-500 mb-8">
          <Link href="/" className="hover:text-white">Home</Link>
          {" / "}
          <Link href="/capabilities" className="hover:text-white">Capabilities</Link>
          {" / "}
          <span className="text-gray-300">{cap.name}</span>
        </nav>

        {/* Header */}
        <div className="mb-12">
          <div className="text-5xl mb-4">{cap.icon}</div>
          <h1 className="text-4xl md:text-5xl font-bold mb-4">
            AI {cap.name} Tools
          </h1>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xl mb-6">{cap.description}</p>

          {/* Quick Stats */}
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-4">
            <div className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-2">
              <span className="text-white font-bold">{tools.length}</span>{" "}
              <span className="text-gray-400 text-sm">Total Tools</span>
            </div>
            <div className="bg-green-500/10 border border-green-500/20 rounded-xl px-4 py-2">
              <span className="text-green-400 font-bold">{freeTools.length}</span>{" "}
              <span className="text-gray-400 text-sm">Free / Freemium</span>
            </div>
            {apiTools.length > 0 && (
              <div className="bg-blue-500/10 border border-blue-500/20 rounded-xl px-4 py-2">
                <span className="text-blue-400 font-bold">{apiTools.length}</span>{" "}
                <span className="text-gray-400 text-sm">With API</span>
              </div>
            )}
            {ossTools.length > 0 && (
              <div className="bg-purple-500/10 border border-purple-500/20 rounded-xl px-4 py-2">
                <span className="text-purple-400 font-bold">{ossTools.length}</span>{" "}
                <span className="text-gray-400 text-sm">Open Source</span>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Tool Grid */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-5">
          {tools.map((tool, i) => (
            <Link
              key={tool.slug}
              href={`/tool/${tool.slug}`}
              className="group bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/10 hover:border-purple-500/40 rounded-xl p-5 transition-all"
            >
              <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-3">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <span className="text-gray-500 text-sm font-bold">#{i + 1}</span>
                  <h2 className="font-bold text-white group-hover:text-purple-400 transition-colors">
                    {tool.name}
                  </h2>
                </div>
                <span
                  className={`text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded-full ${
                    PRICING_COLOR[tool.pricing.toLowerCase()] ?? "bg-white/10 text-gray-400"
                  }`}
                >
                  {tool.pricing}
                </span>
              </div>
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm mb-3 line-clamp-2">
                {tool.description}
              </p>
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★</span>
                  <span className="text-sm text-gray-300">{tool.rating.toFixed(1)}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex gap-2">
                  {tool.has_api && (
                    <span className="text-xs bg-blue-500/10 text-blue-400 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">
                      API
                    </span>
                  )}
                  {tool.is_open_source && (
                    <span className="text-xs bg-purple-500/10 text-purple-400 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">
                      OSS
                    </span>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
            </Link>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Related Workflows */}
        {workflows.length > 0 && (
          <section className="mt-16">
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">
              🔗 Workflows Using {cap.name}
            </h2>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
              {workflows.map((wf) => (
                <Link
                  key={wf.slug}
                  href={`/workflows/${wf.slug}`}
                  className="group bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/10 rounded-xl p-5 transition-all"
                >
                  <h3 className="font-bold text-white group-hover:text-purple-400 transition-colors mb-1">
                    {wf.name}
                  </h3>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm mb-2">{wf.description}</p>
                  <div className="flex gap-2">
                    {wf.steps.slice(0, 4).map((s) => (
                      <span
                        key={s.tool_slug}
                        className="text-xs bg-white/5 text-gray-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full"
                      >
                        {s.tool_name ?? s.tool_slug}
                      </span>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                </Link>
              ))}
            </div>
          </section>
        )}

        {/* SEO Footer */}
        <div className="mt-16 prose prose-invert max-w-none">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white mb-4">
            About AI {cap.name} Tools
          </h2>
          <p className="text-gray-400">
            RunAtlas tracks {tools.length} AI tools with {cap.name.toLowerCase()} capabilities.
            {freeTools.length > 0 &&
              ` ${freeTools.length} offer free tiers so you can get started without paying.`}
            {apiTools.length > 0 &&
              ` ${apiTools.length} provide APIs for developers to integrate into their own applications.`}
            {ossTools.length > 0 &&
              ` ${ossTools.length} are open source and can be self-hosted.`}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </main>
  )
}

import { getCapabilities, getTools } from "@/lib/db"
import Link from "next/link"
import type { Metadata } from "next"

export const revalidate = 86400

export const metadata: Metadata = {
  title: "AI Capability Map — Discover Tools by What They Can Do | RunAtlas",
  description:
    "Explore AI tools organized by capabilities: text generation, image creation, video, voice, coding, automation and more. Find the right tool for any task.",
}

export default function CapabilitiesPage() {
  const capabilities = getCapabilities()
  const tools = getTools()

  const capStats = capabilities
    .map((cap) => {
      const capTools = tools.filter((t) => t.capabilities?.includes(cap.slug))
      const topTools = capTools.sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating).slice(0, 5)
      return { ...cap, toolCount: capTools.length, topTools }
    })
    .sort((a, b) => b.toolCount - a.toolCount)

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-[#0a0a0f] text-white">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-6 py-16">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="text-center mb-14">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 bg-purple-500/10 border border-purple-500/20 rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-purple-400 text-sm mb-4">
            <span>🧠</span> AI Capability Engine
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-4xl md:text-6xl font-bold mb-4 bg-gradient-to-r from-white to-gray-400 bg-clip-text text-transparent">
            AI Capability Map
          </h1>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xl max-w-2xl mx-auto">
            Don&apos;t search for tools — search for capabilities. What do you want AI to do?
          </p>
        </div>

        {/* Capability Grid */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-5">
          {capStats.map((cap) => (
            <Link
              key={cap.slug}
              href={`/capabilities/${cap.slug}`}
              className="group bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/10 hover:border-purple-500/40 rounded-2xl p-6 transition-all duration-300"
            >
              <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-3">
                <div className="text-4xl">{cap.icon}</div>
                <span className="text-xs bg-white/10 text-gray-400 px-2 py-1 rounded-full">
                  {cap.toolCount} tools
                </span>
              </div>
              <h2 className="text-lg font-bold text-white mb-2 group-hover:text-purple-400 transition-colors">
                {cap.name}
              </h2>
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm mb-4">{cap.description}</p>

              {/* Top tools preview */}
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
                {cap.topTools.slice(0, 3).map((tool) => (
                  <span
                    key={tool.slug}
                    className="text-xs bg-white/5 text-gray-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full"
                  >
                    {tool.name}
                  </span>
                ))}
                {cap.toolCount > 3 && (
                  <span className="text-xs text-gray-500 px-1">
                    +{cap.toolCount - 3}
                  </span>
                )}
              </div>
            </Link>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Capability Visualization — Graph-like connections */}
        <section className="mt-20">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-8 text-center">
            How AI Capabilities Connect
          </h2>
          <div className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl p-8">
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-6">
              {capStats.slice(0, 8).map((cap) => (
                <div key={cap.slug} className="text-center">
                  <div className="text-3xl mb-2">{cap.icon}</div>
                  <div className="text-sm font-medium text-white mb-1">{cap.name}</div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-gray-500">{cap.toolCount} tools</div>
                  {/* Connection lines visualization */}
                  <div className="flex justify-center gap-1 mt-2">
                    {cap.topTools.slice(0, 3).map((t) => (
                      <div
                        key={t.slug}
                        className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-purple-500/40"
                        title={t.name}
                      />
                    ))}
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
            <p className="text-center text-gray-500 text-sm mt-6">
              Many tools span multiple capabilities — ChatGPT alone covers text, code, translation and more.
            </p>
          </div>
        </section>

        {/* Multi-capability tools */}
        <section className="mt-16">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">🦄 Most Versatile AI Tools</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-400 mb-8">
            Tools that span the most capabilities — true Swiss Army knives of AI.
          </p>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
            {tools
              .filter((t) => t.capabilities?.length >= 2)
              .sort((a, b) => (b.capabilities?.length ?? 0) - (a.capabilities?.length ?? 0))
              .slice(0, 9)
              .map((tool) => (
                <Link
                  key={tool.slug}
                  href={`/tool/${tool.slug}`}
                  className="group bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/10 rounded-xl p-4 transition-all"
                >
                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                    <span className="font-bold text-white group-hover:text-purple-400 transition-colors">
                      {tool.name}
                    </span>
                    <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★ {tool.rating.toFixed(1)}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
                    {tool.capabilities?.map((cap) => {
                      const capData = capabilities.find((c) => c.slug === cap)
                      return (
                        <span
                          key={cap}
                          className="text-xs bg-purple-500/10 text-purple-400 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full"
                        >
                          {capData?.icon} {capData?.name ?? cap}
                        </span>
                      )
                    })}
                  </div>
                </Link>
              ))}
          </div>
        </section>
      </div>
    </main>
  )
}

import { getToolsByCategory, getCategories } from "@/atlas/tools";
import ToolGrid from "@/components/ToolGrid";
import Link from "next/link";
import { notFound } from "next/navigation";
import { ArrowLeft, Layers, FolderOpen } from "lucide-react";

interface PageProps {
  params: Promise<{ slug: string }>;
}

export async function generateMetadata({ params }: PageProps) {
  const { slug } = await params;
  const categories = await getCategories();
  const cat = categories.find(
    (c: { slug: string }) => c.slug === slug
  );
  if (!cat) return { title: "Category Not Found — RunAtlas" };
  return {
    title: `${cat.name} AI Tools — RunAtlas`,
    description: `Explore ${cat.count}+ AI tools in the ${cat.name} category.`,
  };
}

export default async function CategoryPage({ params }: PageProps) {
  const { slug } = await params;
  const categories = await getCategories();
  const currentCat = categories.find(
    (c: { slug: string }) => c.slug === slug
  );

  if (!currentCat) {
    notFound();
  }

  const tools = await getToolsByCategory(currentCat.name);

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen pt-28 pb-24 px-6">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto">
        {/* Back link */}
        <Link
          href="/"
          className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 text-mist hover:text-gold transition-colors text-sm font-mono mb-10"
        >
          <ArrowLeft className="w-4 h-4" />
          Back to Atlas
        </Link>

        {/* Category header */}
        <div className="animate-fadeUp mb-16">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-4 mb-4">
            <div className="w-14 h-14 bg-teal/10 border border-teal/20 rounded-sm flex items-center justify-center">
              <FolderOpen className="w-7 h-7 text-teal-light" />
            </div>
            <div>
              <span className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-gold block mb-1">
                Category
              </span>
              <h1 className="font-display text-4xl md:text-6xl text-paper">
                {currentCat.name}
              </h1>
            </div>
          </div>
          <p className="text-mist font-mono text-sm mt-4">
            {tools.length} tool{tools.length !== 1 ? "s" : ""} in this category
          </p>
        </div>

        <div className="flex flex-col lg:flex-row gap-12">
          {/* Sidebar: other categories */}
          <aside className="lg:w-64 shrink-0 animate-fadeUp-delay">
            <h3 className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-gold mb-4">
              All Categories
            </h3>
            <nav className="flex flex-row flex-wrap lg:flex-col gap-1">
              {categories.map((cat: { slug: string; name: string; count: number }) => (
                <Link
                  key={cat.slug}
                  href={`/category/${cat.slug}`}
                  className={`flex items-center justify-between px-3 py-2 rounded-sm text-sm transition-colors ${
                    cat.slug === slug
                      ? "bg-gold/10 text-gold border border-gold/20"
                      : "text-mist hover:text-paper hover:bg-paper/5"
                  }`}
                >
                  <span className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <Layers className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                    {cat.name}
                  </span>
                  <span className="font-mono text-xs text-mist/60">
                    {cat.count}
                  </span>
                </Link>
              ))}
            </nav>
          </aside>

          {/* Tool grid */}
          <div className="flex-1 animate-fadeUp-delay2">
            <ToolGrid tools={tools} />
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { getCompanyBySlug, getCompanyTools } from "@/atlas/companies";
import ToolCard from "@/components/ToolCard";
import { notFound } from "next/navigation";
import Link from "next/link";
import { ArrowLeft, MapPin, Calendar, Globe2, Briefcase } from "lucide-react";

export default async function CompanyDetailPage({
  params,
}: {
  params: Promise<{ slug: string }>;
}) {
  const { slug } = await params;
  const company = getCompanyBySlug(slug);

  if (!company) return notFound();

  const tools = getCompanyTools(slug);

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen pt-32 pb-24 px-6">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto">
        {/* Back */}
        <Link
          href="/companies"
          className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 text-mist hover:text-gold transition-colors mb-8 font-mono text-sm"
        >
          <ArrowLeft size={14} />
          All Companies
        </Link>

        {/* Header */}
        <div className="mb-12 animate-fadeUp">
          <span className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-gold block mb-3">
            Company Profile
          </span>
          <h1 className="font-display text-5xl md:text-7xl text-paper mb-4">
            {company.name}
          </h1>
          <p className="text-mist text-lg max-w-2xl mb-6">{company.description}</p>

          {/* Meta */}
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-6 text-sm text-mist">
            <span className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <MapPin size={14} className="text-gold" />
              {company.hq_city}, {company.hq_country}
            </span>
            {company.founded_year > 0 && (
              <span className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <Calendar size={14} className="text-gold" />
                Founded {company.founded_year}
              </span>
            )}
            <span className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <Briefcase size={14} className="text-gold" />
              {tools.length} tool{tools.length !== 1 ? "s" : ""}
            </span>
            {company.website && (
              <a
                href={company.website}
                target="_blank"
                rel="noopener noreferrer"
                className="flex items-center gap-2 hover:text-gold transition-colors"
              >
                <Globe2 size={14} className="text-gold" />
                Website
              </a>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Tools */}
        {tools.length > 0 && (
          <div className="animate-fadeUp-delay">
            <h2 className="font-display text-3xl text-paper mb-6">
              Tools by {company.name}
            </h2>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-6">
              {tools.map((tool) => (
                <ToolCard key={tool.slug} tool={tool} />
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/compare/page.tsx
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

"use client";

import { useSearchParams, useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { useState, useEffect, Suspense } from "react";
import SearchBar from "@/components/SearchBar";
import CompareTable from "@/components/CompareTable";
import FeatureMatrix from "@/components/FeatureMatrix";
import { GitCompareArrows, Plus, X, Search } from "lucide-react";

interface Tool {
  name: string;
  slug: string;
  description: string;
  website: string;
  category: string;
  pricing: string;
  company: string;
  tags: string[];
  rating: number;
  features: string[];
}

function CompareContent() {
  const searchParams = useSearchParams();
  const router = useRouter();
  const initial = searchParams.get("tools")?.split(",").filter(Boolean) || [];
  const [slugs, setSlugs] = useState<string[]>(initial);
  const [tools, setTools] = useState<Tool[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState("");
  const [searchResults, setSearchResults] = useState<Tool[]>([]);
  const [showSearch, setShowSearch] = useState(false);

  // Fetch tools for comparison
  useEffect(() => {
    if (slugs.length === 0) {
      setTools([]);
      return;
    }
    setLoading(true);
    fetch(`/api/compare?slugs=${slugs.join(",")}`)
      .then((res) => res.json())
      .then((data) => {
        setTools(Array.isArray(data) ? data : []);
        setLoading(false);
      })
      .catch(() => setLoading(false));
  }, [slugs]);

  // Search for tools to add
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!searchQuery.trim()) {
      setSearchResults([]);
      return;
    }
    const timer = setTimeout(() => {
      fetch(`/api/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(searchQuery)}`)
        .then((res) => res.json())
        .then((data) => setSearchResults(data.slice(0, 8)))
        .catch(() => setSearchResults([]));
    }, 300);
    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  }, [searchQuery]);

  const addTool = (slug: string) => {
    if (slugs.length >= 4) return;
    if (slugs.includes(slug)) return;
    const next = [...slugs, slug];
    setSlugs(next);
    setSearchQuery("");
    setShowSearch(false);
    router.push(`/compare?tools=${next.join(",")}`);
  };

  const removeTool = (slug: string) => {
    const next = slugs.filter((s) => s !== slug);
    setSlugs(next);
    router.push(`/compare?tools=${next.join(",")}`);
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen pt-32 pb-24 px-6">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="mb-12 animate-fadeUp">
          <span className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-gold block mb-3">
            <GitCompareArrows size={12} className="inline mr-2" />
            Compare
          </span>
          <h1 className="font-display text-5xl md:text-7xl text-paper mb-4">
            Side by Side
          </h1>
          <p className="text-mist text-lg max-w-2xl">
            Compare up to 4 AI tools side by side. Analyze features, pricing, and capabilities.
          </p>
        </div>

        {/* Selected tools + Add */}
        <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-3 mb-8 animate-fadeUp-delay">
          {slugs.map((slug) => (
            <div
              key={slug}
              className="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 bg-surface border border-gold/10 rounded-sm"
            >
              <span className="font-mono text-sm text-paper">{slug.replace(/-/g, " ")}</span>
              <button
                onClick={() => removeTool(slug)}
                className="text-mist/40 hover:text-rust transition-colors"
              >
                <X size={14} />
              </button>
            </div>
          ))}

          {slugs.length < 4 && (
            <div className="relative">
              <button
                onClick={() => setShowSearch(!showSearch)}
                className="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 bg-surface border border-dashed border-gold/20 rounded-sm text-mist hover:text-gold hover:border-gold/40 transition-colors"
              >
                <Plus size={14} />
                <span className="font-mono text-sm">Add tool</span>
              </button>

              {showSearch && (
                <div className="absolute top-full left-0 mt-2 w-80 bg-surface border border-gold/10 rounded-sm shadow-xl z-50">
                  <div className="p-3 border-b border-paper/5">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 bg-ink border border-paper/10 rounded-sm">
                      <Search size={14} className="text-mist" />
                      <input
                        type="text"
                        value={searchQuery}
                        onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
                        placeholder="Search tools..."
                        className="bg-transparent text-paper text-sm outline-none flex-grow font-mono placeholder:text-mist/30"
                        autoFocus
                      />
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  {searchResults.length > 0 && (
                    <div className="max-h-60 overflow-y-auto">
                      {searchResults.map((tool) => (
                        <button
                          key={tool.slug}
                          onClick={() => addTool(tool.slug)}
                          disabled={slugs.includes(tool.slug)}
                          className="w-full text-left px-4 py-3 hover:bg-paper/5 transition-colors border-b border-paper/5 last:border-0 disabled:opacity-30"
                        >
                          <p className="text-sm text-paper">{tool.name}</p>
                          <p className="text-xs text-mist/50 font-mono">{tool.category.replace(/_/g, " ")}</p>
                        </button>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Loading */}
        {loading && (
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center py-20">
            <div className="w-8 h-8 border-2 border-gold/20 border-t-gold rounded-full animate-spin" />
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Compare Table */}
        {!loading && tools.length > 0 && (
          <div className="space-y-10 animate-fadeUp-delay">
            <CompareTable tools={tools} />

            {/* Feature Matrix */}
            <div>
              <h2 className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-gold mb-6">
                Feature Comparison
              </h2>
              <FeatureMatrix tools={tools} />
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Empty state */}
        {!loading && tools.length === 0 && slugs.length === 0 && (
          <div className="text-center py-20 animate-fadeUp-delay">
            <GitCompareArrows size={48} className="text-mist/20 mx-auto mb-6" />
            <h3 className="font-display text-2xl text-paper mb-3">No tools selected</h3>
            <p className="text-mist max-w-md mx-auto">
              Click &quot;Add tool&quot; above to start comparing AI tools side by side.
            </p>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function ComparePage() {
  return (
    <Suspense fallback={
      <div className="min-h-screen pt-32 pb-24 px-6 flex items-center justify-center">
        <div className="w-8 h-8 border-2 border-gold/20 border-t-gold rounded-full animate-spin" />
      </div>
    }>
      <CompareContent />
    </Suspense>
  );
}

import { getToolStats, getCategories, getTopRatedTools, getFeaturedTools } from "@/atlas/tools";
import { getTopCompanies, getCompaniesByCountry } from "@/atlas/companies";
import { getAllWorkflows } from "@/atlas/workflows";
import StatsCard from "@/components/StatsCard";
import Link from "next/link";
import { Layers, Building2, Star, Tags, Globe2, Workflow, TrendingUp, Zap } from "lucide-react";

export const metadata = {
  title: "Dashboard — RunAtlas",
  description: "Analytics and insights about the AI tool ecosystem.",
};

export default function DashboardPage() {
  const stats = getToolStats();
  const categories = getCategories();
  const topRated = getTopRatedTools(10);
  const topCompanies = getTopCompanies(10);
  const byCountry = getCompaniesByCountry();
  const workflows = getAllWorkflows();

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen pt-32 pb-24 px-6">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="mb-12 animate-fadeUp">
          <span className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-gold block mb-3">
            <TrendingUp size={12} className="inline mr-2" />
            Analytics
          </span>
          <h1 className="font-display text-5xl md:text-7xl text-paper mb-4">
            Dashboard
          </h1>
          <p className="text-mist text-lg max-w-2xl">
            Real-time insights into the AI tool ecosystem tracked by RunAtlas.
          </p>
        </div>

        {/* Stats Grid */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4 mb-16 animate-fadeUp-delay">
          <StatsCard label="Total Tools" value={stats.totalTools} icon={Layers} color="gold" />
          <StatsCard label="Companies" value={stats.totalCompanies} icon={Building2} color="teal" />
          <StatsCard label="Categories" value={stats.totalCategories} icon={Tags} color="rust" />
          <StatsCard label="Workflows" value={workflows.length} icon={Workflow} color="mist" />
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-8">
          {/* Category Distribution */}
          <div className="bg-surface border border-gold/5 rounded-sm p-6">
            <h3 className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-gold mb-6">
              Category Distribution
            </h3>
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {categories.map((cat) => {
                const pct = Math.round((cat.count / stats.totalTools) * 100);
                return (
                  <div key={cat.slug}>
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-1">
                      <span className="text-sm text-paper flex items-center gap-2">
                        <span>{cat.icon}</span>
                        {cat.name.replace(/_/g, " ")}
                      </span>
                      <span className="font-mono text-xs text-mist">{cat.count} ({pct}%)</span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="h-1.5 bg-paper/5 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                      <div
                        className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-gold to-gold/50 rounded-full transition-all duration-500"
                        style={{ width: `${pct}%` }}
                      />
                    </div>
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Top Rated */}
          <div className="bg-surface border border-gold/5 rounded-sm p-6">
            <h3 className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-gold mb-6">
              Top Rated Tools
            </h3>
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {topRated.map((tool, i) => (
                <Link
                  key={tool.slug}
                  href={`/tool/${tool.slug}`}
                  className="flex items-center gap-4 p-3 rounded-sm hover:bg-paper/5 transition-colors group"
                >
                  <span className="font-display text-lg text-gold/50 w-6 text-right">{i + 1}</span>
                  <div className="flex-grow">
                    <p className="text-paper text-sm group-hover:text-gold transition-colors">{tool.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-mist/50 text-xs font-mono">{tool.company}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
                    <Star size={12} className="text-gold fill-gold" />
                    <span className="font-mono text-sm text-paper">{tool.rating.toFixed(1)}</span>
                  </div>
                </Link>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Top Companies */}
          <div className="bg-surface border border-gold/5 rounded-sm p-6">
            <h3 className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-gold mb-6">
              Most Prolific Companies

            <div className="space-y-3">

                  key={company.slug}

                  className="flex items-center gap-4 p-3 rounded-sm hover:bg-paper/5 transition-colors group"
                >
                  <span className="font-display text-lg text-gold/50 w-6 text-right">{i + 1}</span>

                        style={{ width: `${Math.max(pct, 2)}%` }}
                      />
                    </div>
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="mt-8 bg-surface border border-gold/5 rounded-sm p-6">
          <h3 className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-gold mb-6">

            Free Tools Available

            </div>
            <div className="flex-grow h-4 bg-paper/5 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
              <div
                className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-teal to-gold rounded-full"
                style={{ width: `${Math.round((stats.freeTools / stats.totalTools) * 100)}%` }}
              />

            <div>
              <p className="font-display text-2xl text-mist">{Math.round((stats.freeTools / stats.totalTools) * 100)}%</p>
              <p className="font-mono text-xs text-mist/60 mt-1">of all tools</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/globals.css
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

@tailwind base;
@tailwind components;
@tailwind utilities;

/* ── Custom Fonts ─────────────────── */
@import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Bebas+Neue&family=DM+Mono:wght@300;400;500&family=DM+Serif+Display&family=Instrument+Sans:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap');

/* ── Base ─────────────────────────── */
@layer base {
  ::selection {
    @apply bg-gold/30 text-paper;
  }
}

/* ── Components ───────────────────── */
@layer components {
  .btn-clip {
    clip-path: polygon(0 0, calc(100% - 8px) 0, 100% 8px, 100% 100%, 8px 100%, 0 calc(100% - 8px));
  }
}

/* ── Animations ───────────────────── */
@keyframes fadeUp {
  from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(20px); }
  to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
}

@keyframes fadeUp-delay {
  0%, 30% { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(20px); }
  100% { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
}

@keyframes float {
  0%, 100% { transform: translateY(0); }
  50% { transform: translateY(-20px); }
}

@keyframes float-delayed {
  0%, 100% { transform: translateY(0); }
  50% { transform: translateY(-15px); }
}

@keyframes marquee {
  from { transform: translateX(0); }
  to { transform: translateX(-33.33%); }
}

@keyframes pulse-slow {
  0%, 100% { opacity: 0.5; }
  50% { opacity: 1; }
}

.animate-fadeUp { animation: fadeUp 0.6s ease-out both; }
.animate-fadeUp-delay { animation: fadeUp-delay 0.9s ease-out both; }
.animate-float { animation: float 6s ease-in-out infinite; }
.animate-float-delayed { animation: float-delayed 8s ease-in-out infinite; }
.animate-marquee { animation: marquee 60s linear infinite; }
.animate-pulse-slow { animation: pulse-slow 3s ease-in-out infinite; }

/* ── Scrollbar ────────────────────── */
::-webkit-scrollbar {
  width: 6px;
  height: 6px;
}

::-webkit-scrollbar-track {
  background: #0a0a0f;
}

::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb {
  background: #c9a84c33;
  border-radius: 3px;
}

::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb:hover {
  background: #c9a84c66;
}

/* ── Utilities ────────────────────── */
.line-clamp-2 {
  display: -webkit-box;
  -webkit-line-clamp: 2;
  -webkit-box-orient: vertical;
  overflow: hidden;
}

.line-clamp-3 {
  display: -webkit-box;
  -webkit-line-clamp: 3;
  -webkit-box-orient: vertical;
  overflow: hidden;
}

import { MetadataRoute } from "next"

export default function robots(): MetadataRoute.Robots {
  return {
    rules: {
      userAgent: "*",
      allow: "/",
      disallow: ["/admin/", "/api/admin/"],
    },
    sitemap: "https://runatlas.com/sitemap.xml",
  }
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/search/page.tsx
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

"use client";

import { useSearchParams } from "next/navigation";
import { useEffect, useState, Suspense } from "react";
import ToolGrid from "@/components/ToolGrid";
import SearchBar from "@/components/SearchBar";
import { Search } from "lucide-react";

interface Tool {
  name: string;
  slug: string;
  description: string;
  website: string;
  category: string;
  pricing: string;
  company: string;
  tags: string[];
  logo: string;
}

function SearchResults() {
  const searchParams = useSearchParams();
  const q = searchParams.get("q") || "";
  const [results, setResults] = useState<Tool[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [searched, setSearched] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!q) {
      setResults([]);
      setSearched(false);
      return;
    }

    const fetchResults = async () => {
      setLoading(true);
      try {
        const res = await fetch(`/api/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(q)}`);
        const data = await res.json();
        setResults(data);
      } catch {
        setResults([]);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
        setSearched(true);
      }
    };

    fetchResults();
  }, [q]);

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen pt-32 pb-24 px-6">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="mb-12 animate-fadeUp">
          <span className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-gold block mb-3">
            Search
          </span>
          <h1 className="font-display text-5xl md:text-6xl text-paper mb-6">
            {q ? (
              <>
                Results for{" "}
                <span className="text-gold">&ldquo;{q}&rdquo;</span>
              </>
            ) : (
              "Search the Atlas"
            )}
          </h1>

          <div className="max-w-2xl">
            <SearchBar />
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Loading */}
        {loading && (
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-6">
            {Array.from({ length: 8 }).map((_, i) => (
              <div
                key={i}
                className="bg-paper/5 border border-paper/10 rounded-sm p-6 animate-pulse"
              >
                <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-paper/10 rounded-sm mb-4" />
                <div className="h-5 bg-paper/10 rounded w-3/4 mb-3" />
                <div className="h-3 bg-paper/10 rounded w-full mb-2" />
                <div className="h-3 bg-paper/10 rounded w-2/3" />
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Results */}
        {!loading && searched && results.length > 0 && (
          <div className="animate-fadeUp-delay">
            <p className="text-mist text-sm mb-8 font-mono">
              {results.length} tool{results.length !== 1 ? "s" : ""} found
            </p>
            <ToolGrid tools={results} />
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Empty state */}
        {!loading && searched && results.length === 0 && q && (
          <div className="text-center py-24 animate-fadeUp-delay">
            <Search className="w-16 h-16 text-mist/30 mx-auto mb-6" />
            <h3 className="font-display text-2xl text-paper mb-3">
              No results found
            </h3>
            <p className="text-mist max-w-md mx-auto">
              No tools matched &ldquo;{q}&rdquo;. Try a different search term or{" "}
              <a href="/submit-tool" className="text-gold hover:underline">
                submit a tool
              </a>{" "}
              we might be missing.
            </p>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Initial state */}
        {!loading && !searched && (
          <div className="text-center py-24 animate-fadeUp-delay">
            <Search className="w-16 h-16 text-mist/30 mx-auto mb-6" />
            <h3 className="font-display text-2xl text-paper mb-3">
              Explore 500+ AI Tools
            </h3>
            <p className="text-mist max-w-md mx-auto">
              Type a keyword, tool name, or category to start searching.
            </p>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function SearchPage() {
  return (
    <Suspense
      fallback={
        <div className="min-h-screen pt-32 pb-24 px-6">
          <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto">
            <div className="h-12 bg-paper/10 rounded w-1/3 animate-pulse" />
          </div>
        </div>
      }
    >
      <SearchResults />
    </Suspense>
  );
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/sitemap.ts

import { MetadataRoute } from "next"
import { getTools, getWorkflows, getUseCases, getCapabilities } from "@/lib/db"

export default function sitemap(): MetadataRoute.Sitemap {
  const BASE_URL = "https://runatlas.com"
  const tools = getTools()
  const workflows = getWorkflows()
  const useCases = getUseCases()
  const capabilities = getCapabilities()

  const SEO_SLUGS = [
    "ai-tools-for-writing",
    "free-ai-tools",
    "ai-tools-for-youtube",
    "ai-tools-for-marketing",
    "ai-coding-tools",
    "ai-image-generators",
    "ai-video-tools",
    "ai-tools-for-students",
    "open-source-ai-tools",
    "ai-voice-tools",
  ]

  const categories = [...new Set(tools.map((t) => t.category))]

  return [
    // Core pages
    { url: BASE_URL, lastModified: new Date(), changeFrequency: "daily", priority: 1 },
    { url: `${BASE_URL}/search`, lastModified: new Date(), changeFrequency: "daily", priority: 0.9 },
    { url: `${BASE_URL}/capabilities`, lastModified: new Date(), changeFrequency: "weekly", priority: 0.9 },
    { url: `${BASE_URL}/use-cases`, lastModified: new Date(), changeFrequency: "weekly", priority: 0.9 },
    { url: `${BASE_URL}/workflows`, lastModified: new Date(), changeFrequency: "weekly", priority: 0.8 },
    { url: `${BASE_URL}/trending`, lastModified: new Date(), changeFrequency: "daily", priority: 0.9 },
    { url: `${BASE_URL}/timeline`, lastModified: new Date(), changeFrequency: "weekly", priority: 0.7 },
    { url: `${BASE_URL}/stack-builder`, lastModified: new Date(), changeFrequency: "monthly", priority: 0.7 },
    { url: `${BASE_URL}/compare`, lastModified: new Date(), changeFrequency: "daily", priority: 0.8 },
    { url: `${BASE_URL}/companies`, lastModified: new Date(), changeFrequency: "weekly", priority: 0.7 },
    { url: `${BASE_URL}/globe`, lastModified: new Date(), changeFrequency: "monthly", priority: 0.6 },
    { url: `${BASE_URL}/graph`, lastModified: new Date(), changeFrequency: "weekly", priority: 0.7 },
    { url: `${BASE_URL}/submit-tool`, lastModified: new Date(), changeFrequency: "monthly", priority: 0.5 },

    // Tool pages
    ...tools.map((t) => ({
      url: `${BASE_URL}/tool/${t.slug}`,
      lastModified: new Date(),
      changeFrequency: "weekly" as const,
      priority: 0.8,
    })),

    // Category pages
    ...categories.map((cat) => ({
      url: `${BASE_URL}/category/${cat}`,
      lastModified: new Date(),
      changeFrequency: "weekly" as const,
      priority: 0.8,
    })),

    // Workflow pages
    ...workflows.map((w) => ({
      url: `${BASE_URL}/workflows/${w.slug}`,
      lastModified: new Date(),
      changeFrequency: "weekly" as const,
      priority: 0.7,
    })),

    // Use case pages
    ...useCases.map((uc) => ({
      url: `${BASE_URL}/use-cases/${uc.slug}`,
      lastModified: new Date(),
      changeFrequency: "weekly" as const,
      priority: 0.8,
    })),

    // Capability pages
    ...capabilities.map((cap) => ({
      url: `${BASE_URL}/capabilities/${cap.slug}`,
      lastModified: new Date(),
      changeFrequency: "weekly" as const,
      priority: 0.8,
    })),

    // SEO pages
    ...SEO_SLUGS.map((slug) => ({
      url: `${BASE_URL}/best/${slug}`,
      lastModified: new Date(),
      changeFrequency: "weekly" as const,
      priority: 0.9,
    })),
  ]
}
