  { id: "design", label: "Design & Creative", icon: "🎨", capability: "design-creative" },
  { id: "data", label: "Data Analysis", icon: "📊", capability: "data-analysis" },
  { id: "marketing", label: "Marketing & SEO", icon: "📈", capability: "seo-marketing" },
]

export default function StackBuilderPage() {
  const [allTools, setAllTools] = useState<Tool[]>([])
  const [stack, setStack] = useState<Record<string, string | null>>({})
  const [expandedSlot, setExpandedSlot] = useState<string | null>(null)
  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState("")

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch("/api/search?q=*&limit=500")
      .then((r) => r.json())
      .then((data) => setAllTools(data.tools || data || []))
      .catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  const getToolsForSlot = useCallback(
    (capability: string) => {
      let filtered = allTools.filter((t) =>
        t.capabilities?.includes(capability)
      )
      if (searchQuery) {
        const q = searchQuery.toLowerCase()
        filtered = filtered.filter(
          (t) =>
            t.name.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
            t.description.toLowerCase().includes(q)
        )
      }
      return filtered.sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating).slice(0, 12)
    },
    [allTools, searchQuery]
  )

  const selectedTools = Object.entries(stack)
    .filter(([, slug]) => slug)
    .map(([slotId, slug]) => {
      const slot = STACK_SLOTS.find((s) => s.id === slotId)
      const tool = allTools.find((t) => t.slug === slug)
      return { slot, tool }
    })
    .filter((s) => s.slot && s.tool)

  const totalCost = selectedTools.reduce((acc, { tool }) => {
    if (tool?.pricing === "free") return acc
    return acc + 1 // placeholder
  }, 0)

  const shareUrl =
    typeof window !== "undefined"
      ? `${window.location.origin}/stack-builder?tools=${selectedTools.map((s) => s.tool?.slug).join(",")}`
      : ""

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-[#0a0a0f] text-white">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-6 py-16">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="text-center mb-14">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 bg-emerald-500/10 border border-emerald-500/20 rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-emerald-400 text-sm mb-4">
            <span>🧰</span> AI Stack Builder
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-4xl md:text-6xl font-bold mb-4 bg-gradient-to-r from-white to-gray-400 bg-clip-text text-transparent">
            Build Your AI Stack
          </h1>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xl max-w-2xl mx-auto">
            Pick the best AI tool for each task. Build your perfect toolkit and share it with others.
          </p>
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-8">
          {/* Stack Slots */}
          <div className="lg:col-span-2 space-y-3">
            {STACK_SLOTS.map((slot) => {
              const selectedSlug = stack[slot.id]
              const selectedTool = selectedSlug
                ? allTools.find((t) => t.slug === selectedSlug)
                : null
              const isExpanded = expandedSlot === slot.id

              return (
                <div
                  key={slot.id}
                  className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl overflow-hidden"
                >
                  {/* Slot Header */}
                  <button
                    onClick={() =>
                      setExpandedSlot(isExpanded ? null : slot.id)
                    }
                    className="w-full flex items-center justify-between p-4 hover:bg-white/5 transition-colors"
                  >
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                      <span className="text-2xl">{slot.icon}</span>
                      <div className="text-left">
                        <div className="font-medium text-white">
                          {slot.label}
                        </div>
                        {selectedTool ? (
                          <div className="text-sm text-emerald-400">
                            {selectedTool.name} — ★{" "}
                            {selectedTool.rating.toFixed(1)}
                          </div>
                        ) : (
                          <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">
                            Click to choose a tool
                          </div>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                      {selectedTool && (
                        <button
                          onClick={(e) => {
                            e.stopPropagation()
                            setStack((prev) => ({
                              ...prev,
                              [slot.id]: null,
                            }))
                          }}
                          className="text-xs text-red-400 hover:text-red-300 px-2 py-1 rounded"
                        >
                          ✕ Remove
                        </button>
                      )}
                      <span className="text-gray-500 text-sm">
                        {isExpanded ? "▲" : "▼"}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                  </button>

                  {/* Expanded Tool Picker */}
                  {isExpanded && (
                    <div className="border-t border-white/10 p-4">
                      <input
                        type="text"
                        placeholder="Search tools..."
                        value={searchQuery}
                        onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
                        className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white placeholder:text-gray-500 mb-3 focus:outline-none focus:border-emerald-500/40"
                      />
                      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-2 max-h-60 overflow-y-auto">
                        {getToolsForSlot(slot.capability).map((tool) => (
                          <button
                            key={tool.slug}
                            onClick={() => {
                              setStack((prev) => ({
                                ...prev,
                                [slot.id]: tool.slug,
                              }))
                              setExpandedSlot(null)
                              setSearchQuery("")
                            }}
                            className={`text-left p-3 rounded-lg border transition-all ${
                              selectedSlug === tool.slug
                                ? "bg-emerald-500/20 border-emerald-500/40 text-emerald-400"
                                : "bg-white/5 border-white/10 hover:bg-white/10 text-white"
                            }`}
                          >
                            <div className="font-medium text-sm">
                              {tool.name}
                            </div>
                            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-1">
                              <span className="text-yellow-400 text-xs">
                                ★ {tool.rating.toFixed(1)}
                              </span>
                              <span className="text-gray-500 text-xs capitalize">
                                {tool.pricing}
                              </span>
                            </div>
                          </button>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              )
            })}
          </div>

          {/* Stack Summary Sidebar */}
          <div className="space-y-6">
            <div className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl p-6 sticky top-20">
              <h2 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">Your AI Stack</h2>

              {selectedTools.length === 0 ? (
                <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm">
                  Pick tools from the left to build your stack.
                </p>
              ) : (
                <>
                  <div className="space-y-3 mb-6">
                    {selectedTools.map(({ slot, tool }) => (
                      <div
                        key={slot!.id}
                        className="flex items-center gap-3 p-3 bg-white/5 rounded-lg"
                      >
                        <span className="text-lg">{slot!.icon}</span>
                        <div>
                          <Link
                            href={`/tool/${tool!.slug}`}
                            className="text-sm font-medium text-white hover:text-emerald-400 transition-colors"
                          >
                            {tool!.name}
                          </Link>
                          <div className="text-xs text-gray-500">
                            {slot!.label}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </div>

                  <div className="border-t border-white/10 pt-4 mb-4">
                    <div className="flex justify-between text-sm mb-1">
                      <span className="text-gray-400">Tools selected</span>
                      <span className="text-white font-bold">
                        {selectedTools.length}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                      <span className="text-gray-400">Free tools</span>
                      <span className="text-green-400">
                        {
                          selectedTools.filter(
                            (s) =>
                              s.tool?.pricing === "free" ||
                              s.tool?.pricing === "freemium"
                          ).length
                        }
                      </span>
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  <button
                    onClick={() => {
                      if (navigator.clipboard) {
                        navigator.clipboard.writeText(shareUrl)
                        alert("Stack link copied to clipboard!")
                      }
                    }}
                    className="w-full py-2 px-4 bg-emerald-600 hover:bg-emerald-500 text-white rounded-xl font-medium transition-colors text-sm"
                  >
                    📋 Copy Stack Link
                  </button>
                </>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </main>
  )
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/submit-tool/page.tsx
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

"use client";

import { useState, useEffect } from "react";
import { Send, CheckCircle, AlertCircle, ArrowLeft } from "lucide-react";
import Link from "next/link";

const CATEGORY_OPTIONS = [
  "AI Assistants",
  "Image Generation",
  "Text Generation",
  "Code Generation",
  "Video Generation",
  "Audio & Music",
  "Data Analysis",
  "Automation",
  "Productivity",
  "Marketing",
  "Design",
  "Research",
  "Education",
  "Healthcare",
  "Finance",
  "Legal",
  "Customer Support",
  "Developer Tools",
];

export default function SubmitToolPage() {
  const [form, setForm] = useState({
    name: "",
    website: "",
    description: "",
    category: "",
    company: "",
  });
  const [status, setStatus] = useState<"idle" | "loading" | "success" | "error">("idle");
  const [errorMsg, setErrorMsg] = useState("");

  const handleChange = (
    e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement | HTMLSelectElement>
  ) => {
    setForm((prev) => ({ ...prev, [e.target.name]: e.target.value }));
  };

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setStatus("loading");
    setErrorMsg("");

    try {
      const res = await fetch("/api/submit", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(form),
      });
      const data = await res.json();

      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error(data.error || "Failed to submit");
      }

      setStatus("success");
      setForm({ name: "", website: "", description: "", category: "", company: "" });
    } catch (err: any) {
      setStatus("error");
      setErrorMsg(err.message || "Something went wrong");
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen pt-28 pb-24 px-6">
      <div className="max-w-2xl mx-auto">
        {/* Back link */}
        <Link
          href="/"
          className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 text-mist hover:text-gold transition-colors text-sm font-mono mb-10"
        >
          <ArrowLeft className="w-4 h-4" />
          Back to Atlas
        </Link>

        <div className="animate-fadeUp">
          <span className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-gold block mb-3">
            Contribute
          </span>
          <h1 className="font-display text-5xl md:text-6xl text-paper mb-4">
            Submit a Tool
          </h1>
          <p className="text-mist text-lg mb-12">
            Know an AI tool that&apos;s missing from the atlas? Submit it here
            and help the community discover great tools.
          </p>
        </div>

        {/* Success state */}
        {status === "success" && (
          <div className="bg-teal/10 border border-teal/30 rounded-sm p-8 text-center animate-fadeUp">
            <CheckCircle className="w-12 h-12 text-teal-light mx-auto mb-4" />
            <h3 className="font-display text-2xl text-paper mb-2">
              Tool Submitted!
            </h3>
            <p className="text-mist">
              Thank you for your contribution. We&apos;ll review your submission
              and add it to the atlas.
            </p>
            <button
              onClick={() => setStatus("idle")}
              className="mt-6 text-gold hover:underline font-mono text-sm"
            >
              Submit another tool
            </button>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Form */}
        {status !== "success" && (
          <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-6 animate-fadeUp-delay">
            {/* Error banner */}
            {status === "error" && (
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3 bg-rust/10 border border-rust/30 rounded-sm p-4">
                <AlertCircle className="w-5 h-5 text-rust shrink-0" />
                <p className="text-rust text-sm">{errorMsg}</p>
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Name */}
            <div>
              <label className="block font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-mist mb-2">
                Tool Name *
              </label>
              <input
                type="text"
                name="name"
                value={form.name}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
                placeholder="e.g. ChatGPT"
                className="w-full bg-paper/5 border border-paper/10 rounded-sm px-4 py-3 text-paper placeholder:text-mist/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-gold/60 focus:ring-1 focus:ring-gold/30 transition-colors"
              />
            </div>

            {/* Website */}
            <div>
              <label className="block font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-mist mb-2">
                Website URL *
              </label>
              <input
                type="url"
                name="website"
                value={form.website}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
                placeholder="https://example.com"
                className="w-full bg-paper/5 border border-paper/10 rounded-sm px-4 py-3 text-paper placeholder:text-mist/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-gold/60 focus:ring-1 focus:ring-gold/30 transition-colors"
              />
            </div>

            {/* Description */}
            <div>
              <label className="block font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-mist mb-2">
                Description *
              </label>
              <textarea
                name="description"
                value={form.description}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
                rows={4}
                placeholder="What does this tool do?"
                className="w-full bg-paper/5 border border-paper/10 rounded-sm px-4 py-3 text-paper placeholder:text-mist/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-gold/60 focus:ring-1 focus:ring-gold/30 transition-colors resize-none"
              />
            </div>

            {/* Category */}
            <div>
              <label className="block font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-mist mb-2">
                Category *
              </label>
              <select
                name="category"
                value={form.category}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
                className="w-full bg-paper/5 border border-paper/10 rounded-sm px-4 py-3 text-paper focus:outline-none focus:border-gold/60 focus:ring-1 focus:ring-gold/30 transition-colors appearance-none"
              >
                <option value="" className="bg-ink">
                  Select a category
                </option>
                {CATEGORY_OPTIONS.map((cat) => (
                  <option key={cat} value={cat} className="bg-ink">
                    {cat}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>

            {/* Company */}
            <div>
              <label className="block font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-mist mb-2">
                Company
              </label>
              <input
                type="text"
                name="company"
                value={form.company}
                onChange={handleChange}
                placeholder="e.g. OpenAI"
                className="w-full bg-paper/5 border border-paper/10 rounded-sm px-4 py-3 text-paper placeholder:text-mist/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-gold/60 focus:ring-1 focus:ring-gold/30 transition-colors"
              />
            </div>

            {/* Submit button */}
            <button
              type="submit"
              disabled={status === "loading"}
              className="btn-clip w-full bg-gold text-ink px-8 py-4 font-semibold text-sm uppercase tracking-wider hover:bg-gold-light transition-colors disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed flex items-center justify-center gap-2"
            >
              {status === "loading" ? (
                <>
                  <span className="w-4 h-4 border-2 border-ink/30 border-t-ink rounded-full animate-spin" />
                  Submitting...
                </>
              ) : (
                <>
                  <Send className="w-4 h-4" />
                  Submit Tool
                </>
              )}
            </button>
          </form>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/timeline/page.tsx
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

import { getTools } from "@/lib/db"
import Link from "next/link"
import type { Metadata } from "next"

export const revalidate = 86400

export const metadata: Metadata = {
  title: "AI Tool Timeline — History of AI Tools | RunAtlas",
  description:
    "Explore the timeline of AI tools from early chatbots to today's multimodal models. See when every major AI tool launched.",
}

// Major AI milestones for context
const MILESTONES = [
  { year: 2020, event: "GPT-3 released", icon: "🧠" },
  { year: 2021, event: "GitHub Copilot preview", icon: "💻" },
  { year: 2022, event: "Stable Diffusion & ChatGPT", icon: "🎨" },
  { year: 2023, event: "GPT-4 & AI video explosion", icon: "🚀" },
  { year: 2024, event: "Multimodal AI & AI agents", icon: "🤖" },
  { year: 2025, event: "AI reasoning & autonomy", icon: "⚡" },
]

// Hardcoded launch dates for major tools (founded_year may differ from launch)
const TOOL_LAUNCHES: Record<string, { year: number; month?: string; event?: string }> = {
  chatgpt: { year: 2022, month: "Nov", event: "ChatGPT launches — AI goes mainstream" },
  "dall-e-3": { year: 2023, month: "Oct", event: "DALL·E 3 released by OpenAI" },
  "stable-diffusion-3": { year: 2024, month: "Feb", event: "Stable Diffusion 3 announced" },
  midjourney: { year: 2022, month: "Jul", event: "Midjourney enters open beta" },
  claude: { year: 2023, month: "Mar", event: "Anthropic releases Claude" },
  gemini: { year: 2023, month: "Dec", event: "Google launches Gemini" },
  "runway-ml": { year: 2023, month: "Feb", event: "Runway Gen-2 video generation" },
  pika: { year: 2023, month: "Nov", event: "Pika 1.0 launches" },
  sora: { year: 2024, month: "Feb", event: "OpenAI previews Sora video model" },
  elevenlabs: { year: 2023, month: "Jan", event: "ElevenLabs voice cloning goes viral" },
  suno: { year: 2023, month: "Dec", event: "Suno AI music generation launches" },
  cursor: { year: 2023, month: "Mar", event: "Cursor AI-first code editor" },
  "github-copilot": { year: 2021, month: "Jun", event: "GitHub Copilot technical preview" },
  perplexity: { year: 2022, month: "Dec", event: "Perplexity AI search launches" },
  "v0-by-vercel": { year: 2023, month: "Oct", event: "v0 by Vercel — AI UI generation" },
  flux: { year: 2024, month: "Aug", event: "Flux image model by Black Forest Labs" },
  "kling-ai": { year: 2024, month: "Jun", event: "Kling AI video from China" },
  "luma-ai": { year: 2024, month: "Jun", event: "Luma Dream Machine video model" },
  heygen: { year: 2023, month: "May", event: "HeyGen AI avatar videos" },
  "bolt-new": { year: 2024, month: "Sep", event: "Bolt.new — AI full-stack builder" },
}

export default function TimelinePage() {
  const tools = getTools()
  const toolsBySlug = Object.fromEntries(tools.map((t) => [t.slug, t]))

  // Build timeline entries
  interface TimelineEntry {
    year: number
    month?: string
    type: "tool" | "milestone"
    name: string
    description: string
    slug?: string
    icon?: string
    rating?: number
  }

  const entries: TimelineEntry[] = []

  // Add milestones
  for (const m of MILESTONES) {
    entries.push({
      year: m.year,
      type: "milestone",
      name: m.event,
      description: "",
      icon: m.icon,
    })
  }

  // Add known launch dates
  for (const [slug, launch] of Object.entries(TOOL_LAUNCHES)) {
    const tool = toolsBySlug[slug]
    if (tool) {
      entries.push({
        year: launch.year,
        month: launch.month,
        type: "tool",
        name: tool.name,
        description: launch.event || tool.description,
        slug: tool.slug,
        rating: tool.rating,
      })
    }
  }

  // Add other tools by founded_year that aren't already covered
  const coveredSlugs = new Set(Object.keys(TOOL_LAUNCHES))
  for (const tool of tools) {
    if (!coveredSlugs.has(tool.slug) && tool.founded_year && tool.founded_year >= 2020) {
      entries.push({
        year: tool.founded_year,
        type: "tool",
        name: tool.name,
        description: tool.description,
        slug: tool.slug,
        rating: tool.rating,
      })
    }
  }

  // Group by year, sort descending
  const years = [...new Set(entries.map((e) => e.year))].sort((a, b) => b - a)

  const yearGroups = years.map((year) => ({
    year,
    entries: entries
      .filter((e) => e.year === year)
      .sort((a, b) => {
        // Milestones first within a year
        if (a.type !== b.type) return a.type === "milestone" ? -1 : 1
        return (b.rating ?? 0) - (a.rating ?? 0)
      }),
  }))

  // Stats
  const totalTimelineTools = entries.filter((e) => e.type === "tool").length
  const yearCounts = yearGroups.map((g) => ({
    year: g.year,
    count: g.entries.filter((e) => e.type === "tool").length,
  }))

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-[#0a0a0f] text-white">
      <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-6 py-16">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="text-center mb-14">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 bg-amber-500/10 border border-amber-500/20 rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-amber-400 text-sm mb-4">
            <span>⏳</span> AI History
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-4xl md:text-6xl font-bold mb-4 bg-gradient-to-r from-white to-gray-400 bg-clip-text text-transparent">
            AI Tool Timeline
          </h1>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xl max-w-2xl mx-auto">
            The history of AI tools — from GPT-3 to today&apos;s multimodal AI revolution.
            {totalTimelineTools} tools tracked.
          </p>
        </div>

        {/* Year distribution bar */}
        <div className="flex items-end gap-2 justify-center mb-12 h-24">
          {yearCounts
            .sort((a, b) => a.year - b.year)
            .map((yc) => {
              const maxCount = Math.max(...yearCounts.map((y) => y.count))
              const height = Math.max(8, (yc.count / maxCount) * 80)
              return (
                <div key={yc.year} className="flex flex-col items-center gap-1">
                  <span className="text-xs text-gray-500">{yc.count}</span>
                  <div
                    className="w-12 bg-gradient-to-t from-amber-600 to-amber-400 rounded-t-lg transition-all"
                    style={{ height: `${height}px` }}
                  />
                  <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">{yc.year}</span>
                </div>
              )
            })}
        </div>

        {/* Timeline */}
        <div className="relative">
          <div className="absolute left-6 top-0 bottom-0 w-px bg-white/10" />

          {yearGroups.map((group) => (
            <div key={group.year} className="mb-12">
              {/* Year marker */}
              <div className="flex items-center gap-4 mb-6">
                <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-full bg-amber-500/20 border-2 border-amber-500/40 flex items-center justify-center text-amber-400 font-bold z-10">
                  {group.year.toString().slice(2)}
                </div>
                <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">{group.year}</h2>
                <span className="text-sm text-gray-500">
                  {group.entries.filter((e) => e.type === "tool").length} tools
                </span>
              </div>

              <div className="ml-14 space-y-3">
                {group.entries.slice(0, 20).map((entry, i) => (
                  <div key={`${entry.name}-${i}`}>
                    {entry.type === "milestone" ? (
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 p-3 bg-amber-500/10 border border-amber-500/20 rounded-xl">
                        <span className="text-xl">{entry.icon}</span>
                        <span className="font-medium text-amber-400">
                          {entry.name}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    ) : (
                      <Link
                        href={`/tool/${entry.slug}`}
                        className="group flex items-start gap-3 p-3 bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/10 hover:border-amber-500/30 rounded-xl transition-all"
                      >
                        <div className="flex-1">
                          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                            {entry.month && (
                              <span className="text-xs text-gray-500 font-mono">
                                {entry.month}
                              </span>
                            )}
                            <span className="font-bold text-white group-hover:text-amber-400 transition-colors">
                              {entry.name}
                            </span>
                            {entry.rating && (
                              <span className="text-yellow-400 text-xs">
                                ★ {entry.rating.toFixed(1)}
                              </span>
                            )}
                          </div>
                          <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm line-clamp-1">
                            {entry.description}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                      </Link>
                    )}
                  </div>
                ))}
                {group.entries.length > 20 && (
                  <div className="text-sm text-gray-500 p-2">
                    +{group.entries.length - 20} more tools in {group.year}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </main>
  )
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/tool/[slug]/page.tsx

import { getTools, getWorkflows, getToolBySlug, getCapabilities } from "@/lib/db"
import { getAlternatives } from "@/atlas/search"
import { notFound } from "next/navigation"
import Link from "next/link"
import type { Metadata } from "next"

export const revalidate = 86400

export async function generateStaticParams() {
  const tools = getTools()
  return tools.map((t) => ({ slug: t.slug }))
}

export async function generateMetadata({ params }: { params: { slug: string } }): Promise<Metadata> {
  const tool = getToolBySlug(params.slug)
  if (!tool) return {}
  return {
    title: `${tool.name} — AI Tool Review, Pricing & Alternatives | RunAtlas`,
    description: tool.description,
    openGraph: { title: tool.name, description: tool.description },
  }
}

export default function ToolDetailPage({ params }: { params: { slug: string } }) {
  const tool = getToolBySlug(params.slug)
  if (!tool) notFound()

  const alternatives = getAlternatives(tool, 6)
  const workflows = getWorkflows().filter((w) =>
    w.steps.some((s) => s.tool_slug === tool.slug)
  )
  const capabilities = getCapabilities()
  const toolCaps = capabilities.filter((c) => tool.capabilities?.includes(c.slug))

  const PRICING_COLOR: Record<string, string> = {
    free: "bg-green-500/20 text-green-400 border-green-500/30",
    freemium: "bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400 border-blue-500/30",
    paid: "bg-orange-500/20 text-orange-400 border-orange-500/30",
    open_source: "bg-purple-500/20 text-purple-400 border-purple-500/30",
  }

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-[#0a0a0f] text-white">
      <div className="max-w-5xl mx-auto px-6 py-12">
        {/* Breadcrumb */}
        <nav className="text-sm text-gray-500 mb-8">
          <Link href="/" className="hover:text-white">Home</Link>
          {" / "}
          <Link href={`/category/${tool.category}`} className="hover:text-white capitalize">
            {tool.category.replace(/_/g, " ")}
          </Link>
          {" / "}
          <span className="text-gray-300">{tool.name}</span>
        </nav>

        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-start gap-6 mb-10">
          <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-2xl bg-white/10 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl flex-shrink-0">
            {tool.name.charAt(0)}
          </div>
          <div className="flex-1">
            <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-3 mb-2">
              <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold">{tool.name}</h1>
              <span className={`text-xs px-3 py-1 rounded-full border ${PRICING_COLOR[tool.pricing.toLowerCase()] ?? "bg-white/10 text-gray-400 border-white/20"}`}>
                {tool.pricing}
              </span>
              {tool.has_api && (
                <span className="text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded-full bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400 border border-blue-500/30">
                  API
                </span>
              )}
              {tool.is_open_source && (
                <span className="text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded-full bg-purple-500/20 text-purple-400 border border-purple-500/30">
                  Open Source
                </span>
              )}
            </div>
            <p className="text-gray-400 text-lg mb-4">{tool.description}</p>

            {/* Capability badges */}
            {toolCaps.length > 0 && (
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-4">
                {toolCaps.map((cap) => (
                  <Link
                    key={cap.slug}
                    href={`/capabilities/${cap.slug}`}
                    className="text-xs bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 text-gray-300 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full border border-white/10 transition-colors"
                  >
                    {cap.icon} {cap.name}
                  </Link>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}

            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3">
              <a
                href={tool.website}
                target="_blank"
                rel="noopener noreferrer"
                className="px-5 py-2 bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white rounded-xl font-medium transition-colors text-sm"
              >
                Visit {tool.name} →
              </a>
              <Link
                href={`/compare?tools=${tool.slug}`}
                className="px-5 py-2 bg-white/10 hover:bg-white/20 text-white rounded-xl font-medium transition-colors text-sm"
              >
                Compare Tools
              </Link>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-8">
          {/* Main content */}
          <div className="lg:col-span-2 space-y-8">
            {/* Description */}
            <section className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl p-6">
              <h2 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">About {tool.name}</h2>
              <p className="text-gray-300 leading-relaxed">
                {tool.long_description || tool.description}
              </p>
            </section>

            {/* Features */}
            {tool.features && tool.features.length > 0 && (
              <section className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl p-6">
                <h2 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">✨ Key Features</h2>
                <ul className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                  {tool.features.map((feature) => (
                    <li key={feature} className="flex items-start gap-2 text-gray-300">
                      <span className="text-green-400 mt-1 flex-shrink-0">✓</span>
                      <span>{feature}</span>
                    </li>
                  ))}
                </ul>
              </section>
            )}

            {/* Pricing Details */}
            <section className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl p-6">
              <h2 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">💰 Pricing</h2>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
                <div className="text-center p-3 bg-white/5 rounded-xl">
                  <div className="text-lg mb-1">
                    {tool.pricing_details?.free_tier ? "✅" : "❌"}
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-gray-400">Free Tier</div>
                </div>
                <div className="text-center p-3 bg-white/5 rounded-xl">
                  <div className="text-sm font-bold text-white mb-1">
                    {tool.pricing_details?.starting_price || "N/A"}
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-gray-400">Starting Price</div>
                </div>
                <div className="text-center p-3 bg-white/5 rounded-xl">
                  <div className="text-lg mb-1">
                    {tool.pricing_details?.enterprise ? "✅" : "❌"}
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-gray-400">Enterprise</div>
                </div>
                <div className="text-center p-3 bg-white/5 rounded-xl">
                  <div className="text-lg mb-1">
                    {tool.has_api ? "✅" : "❌"}
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-gray-400">API Access</div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </section>

            {/* Platforms */}
            {tool.platforms && tool.platforms.length > 0 && (
              <section>
                <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-3 text-gray-400">Available On</h2>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                  {tool.platforms.map((platform) => (
                    <span
                      key={platform}
                      className="text-sm bg-white/5 text-gray-300 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg border border-white/10 capitalize"
                    >
                      {platform === "web" && "🌐 "}
                      {platform === "ios" && "📱 "}
                      {platform === "android" && "🤖 "}
                      {platform === "desktop" && "🖥️ "}
                      {platform === "api" && "⚡ "}
                      {platform === "ide-extension" && "🔌 "}
                      {platform === "browser-extension" && "🧩 "}
                      {platform === "cli" && "⌨️ "}
                      {platform === "slack" && "💬 "}
                      {platform === "discord" && "🎮 "}
                      {platform.replace(/-/g, " ")}
                    </span>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </section>
            )}

            {/* Tags */}
            {tool.tags && tool.tags.length > 0 && (
              <section>
                <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-3 text-gray-400">Tags</h2>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                  {tool.tags.map((tag) => (
                    <span key={tag} className="text-sm bg-white/5 text-gray-300 px-3 py-1 rounded-full border border-white/10">
                      #{tag}
                    </span>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </section>
            )}

            {/* Workflows using this tool */}
            {workflows.length > 0 && (
              <section className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl p-6">
                <h2 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">🔗 Used in Workflows</h2>
                <div className="space-y-3">
                  {workflows.map((wf) => (
                    <Link
                      key={wf.slug}
                      href={`/workflows/${wf.slug}`}
                      className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/10 rounded-xl transition-all group"
                    >
                      <div>
                        <div className="font-medium text-white group-hover:text-indigo-400 transition-colors">
                          {wf.name}
                        </div>
                        <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">{wf.use_case}</div>
                      </div>
                      <span className="text-indigo-400 text-sm">View →</span>
                    </Link>

                <div className="flex justify-between">

                  {tool.company_slug ? (
                    <Link href={`/companies/${tool.company_slug}`} className="text-indigo-400 hover:underline">
                      {tool.company || "Independent"}

                  ) : (
                    <span className="text-white">{tool.company || "Independent"}</span>
                  )}
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between">
                  <span className="text-gray-500">Category</span>
                  <Link href={`/category/${tool.category}`} className="text-indigo-400 hover:underline capitalize">
                    {tool.category.replace(/_/g, " ")}
                  </Link>

                  </div>

                  <div className="flex justify-between">

              </div>
            </div>

            {alternatives.length > 0 && (
              <div className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl p-5">

                  Alternatives to {tool.name}
                </h3>
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  {alternatives.map((alt) => (
                    <Link
                      key={alt.slug}
                      href={`/tool/${alt.slug}`}
                      className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 rounded-xl transition-all group text-sm"
                    >
                      <span className="text-white group-hover:text-indigo-400 transition-colors">
                        {alt.name}
                      </span>
                      <span className="text-gray-500">⭐ {alt.rating.toFixed(1)}</span>
                    </Link>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Capabilities */}
            {toolCaps.length > 0 && (
              <div className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl p-5">
                <h3 className="font-bold mb-4 text-gray-300">Capabilities</h3>

                  ))}

            )}

        </div>
      </div>

  )
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./app/trending/page.tsx
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

import { getTools, getCapabilities } from "@/lib/db"
import { getTrendingTools } from "@/atlas/search"
import Link from "next/link"
import type { Metadata } from "next"

export const revalidate = 86400

export const metadata: Metadata = {
  title: "Trending AI Tools — What's Hot in AI Right Now | RunAtlas",
  description:
    "See the most popular and fastest-growing AI tools. Updated daily with trending tools across every category.",
}

export default function TrendingPage() {
  const allTools = getTools()
  const capabilities = getCapabilities()
  const trending = getTrendingTools(20)

  // Category stats
  const categories = [...new Set(allTools.map((t) => t.category))]
  const categoryStats = categories
    .map((cat) => {
      const catTools = allTools.filter((t) => t.category === cat)
      return {
        name: cat.replace(/_/g, " "),
        slug: cat,
        count: catTools.length,
        avgRating: catTools.reduce((s, t) => s + t.rating, 0) / catTools.length,
        topTool: catTools.sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating)[0],
      }
    })
    .sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count)

  // Pricing distribution
  const pricingDist = {
    free: allTools.filter((t) => t.pricing === "free").length,
    freemium: allTools.filter((t) => t.pricing === "freemium").length,
    paid: allTools.filter((t) => t.pricing === "paid").length,
    open_source: allTools.filter((t) => t.pricing === "open_source" || t.is_open_source).length,
  }

  // Top rated overall
  const topRated = [...allTools].sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating).slice(0, 10)

  // Newest tools (by founded_year)
  const newestTools = [...allTools]
    .filter((t) => t.founded_year && t.founded_year >= 2024)
    .sort((a, b) => (b.founded_year ?? 0) - (a.founded_year ?? 0))
    .slice(0, 10)

  // Open source rising stars
  const ossStars = allTools
    .filter((t) => t.is_open_source)
    .sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating)
    .slice(0, 6)

  const PRICING_COLOR: Record<string, string> = {
    free: "bg-green-500/20 text-green-400",
    freemium: "bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400",
    paid: "bg-orange-500/20 text-orange-400",
    open_source: "bg-purple-500/20 text-purple-400",
  }

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-[#0a0a0f] text-white">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-6 py-16">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="text-center mb-14">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 bg-rose-500/10 border border-rose-500/20 rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-rose-400 text-sm mb-4">
            <span>🔥</span> AI Trends
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-4xl md:text-6xl font-bold mb-4 bg-gradient-to-r from-white to-gray-400 bg-clip-text text-transparent">
            AI Trend Dashboard
          </h1>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xl max-w-2xl mx-auto">
            What&apos;s hot in AI right now. {allTools.length} tools tracked across{" "}
            {categories.length} categories.
          </p>
        </div>

        {/* Key Stats */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4 mb-12">
          <div className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl p-5 text-center">
            <div className="text-3xl font-bold text-white">{allTools.length}</div>
            <div className="text-gray-400 text-sm">AI Tools</div>
          </div>
          <div className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl p-5 text-center">
            <div className="text-3xl font-bold text-green-400">{pricingDist.free + pricingDist.freemium}</div>
            <div className="text-gray-400 text-sm">Free / Freemium</div>
          </div>
          <div className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl p-5 text-center">
            <div className="text-3xl font-bold text-purple-400">{pricingDist.open_source}</div>
            <div className="text-gray-400 text-sm">Open Source</div>
          </div>
          <div className="bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl p-5 text-center">
            <div className="text-3xl font-bold text-blue-400">{categories.length}</div>
            <div className="text-gray-400 text-sm">Categories</div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Trending Tools */}
        <section className="mb-16">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">🔥 Trending Right Now</h2>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
            {trending.map((tool, i) => (
              <Link
                key={tool.slug}
                href={`/tool/${tool.slug}`}
                className="group bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/10 hover:border-rose-500/40 rounded-xl p-4 transition-all"
              >
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                  <span className="text-rose-400 font-bold text-sm">#{i + 1}</span>
                  <span className="font-bold text-white group-hover:text-rose-400 transition-colors">
                    {tool.name}
                  </span>
                </div>
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs line-clamp-2 mb-2">
                  {tool.description}
                </p>
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                  <span className="text-yellow-400 text-xs">★ {tool.rating.toFixed(1)}</span>
                  <span
                    className={`text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${
                      PRICING_COLOR[tool.pricing.toLowerCase()] ?? "bg-white/10 text-gray-400"
                    }`}
                  >
                    {tool.pricing}
                  </span>
                </div>
              </Link>
            ))}
          </div>
        </section>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-12">
          {/* Top Rated */}
          <section>
            <h2 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">⭐ Highest Rated</h2>
            <div className="space-y-2">
              {topRated.map((tool, i) => (
                <Link
                  key={tool.slug}
                  href={`/tool/${tool.slug}`}
                  className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/10 rounded-lg transition-all group"
                >
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <span className="text-gray-500 text-sm w-6">#{i + 1}</span>
                    <span className="text-white group-hover:text-indigo-400 transition-colors font-medium">
                      {tool.name}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★ {tool.rating.toFixed(1)}</span>
                </Link>
              ))}
            </div>
          </section>

          {/* New Launches 2024+ */}
          <section>
            <h2 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">🆕 Newest AI Tools</h2>
            <div className="space-y-2">
              {newestTools.map((tool) => (
                <Link
                  key={tool.slug}
                  href={`/tool/${tool.slug}`}
                  className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/10 rounded-lg transition-all group"
                >
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <span className="text-emerald-400 text-xs font-mono">
                      {tool.founded_year}
                    </span>
                    <span className="text-white group-hover:text-emerald-400 transition-colors font-medium">
                      {tool.name}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★ {tool.rating.toFixed(1)}</span>
                </Link>
              ))}
            </div>
          </section>
        </div>

        {/* Category Breakdown */}
        <section className="mt-16">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">📊 Category Breakdown</h2>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
            {categoryStats.map((cat) => (
              <Link
                key={cat.slug}
                href={`/category/${cat.slug}`}
                className="group bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/10 rounded-xl p-4 transition-all"
              >
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                  <h3 className="font-bold text-white capitalize group-hover:text-indigo-400 transition-colors">
                    {cat.name}
                  </h3>
                  <span className="text-gray-400 text-sm">{cat.count} tools</span>
                </div>
                {/* Bar visualization */}
                <div className="w-full bg-white/5 rounded-full h-2 mb-2">
                  <div
                    className="bg-gradient-to-r from-indigo-500 to-purple-500 h-2 rounded-full transition-all"
                    style={{
                      width: `${(cat.count / categoryStats[0].count) * 100}%`,
                    }}
                  />
                </div>
                {cat.topTool && (
                  <div className="text-xs text-gray-500">
                    Top: {cat.topTool.name} (★ {cat.topTool.rating.toFixed(1)})
                  </div>
                )}
              </Link>
            ))}
          </div>
        </section>

        {/* Open Source Rising Stars */}
        {ossStars.length > 0 && (
          <section className="mt-16">
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">🌟 Open Source Rising Stars</h2>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
              {ossStars.map((tool) => (
                <Link
                  key={tool.slug}
                  href={`/tool/${tool.slug}`}
                  className="group bg-purple-500/5 hover:bg-purple-500/10 border border-purple-500/20 rounded-xl p-5 transition-all"
                >
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                    <span className="font-bold text-white group-hover:text-purple-400 transition-colors">
                      {tool.name}
                    </span>
                    <span className="text-xs bg-purple-500/20 text-purple-400 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">
                      Open Source
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm line-clamp-2">{tool.description}</p>
                </Link>
              ))}
            </div>
          </section>
        )}
      </div>
    </main>
  )
}

import { getUseCases, getTools, getWorkflows } from "@/lib/db"
import { notFound } from "next/navigation"
import Link from "next/link"

export const revalidate = 86400

export async function generateStaticParams() {
  const useCases = getUseCases()
  return useCases.map((uc) => ({ slug: uc.slug }))
}

export default function UseCaseDetailPage({ params }: { params: { slug: string } }) {
  const useCases = getUseCases()
  const uc = useCases.find((u) => u.slug === params.slug)
  if (!uc) notFound()

  const tools = getTools()
  const workflows = getWorkflows()
  const toolsBySlug = Object.fromEntries(tools.map((t) => [t.slug, t]))
  const workflow = uc.workflow_slug ? workflows.find((w) => w.slug === uc.workflow_slug) : null
  const ucTools = uc.tool_slugs.map((s) => toolsBySlug[s]).filter(Boolean)

  const PRICING_COLOR: Record<string, string> = {
    free: "bg-green-500/20 text-green-400",
    freemium: "bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400",
    paid: "bg-orange-500/20 text-orange-400",
    open_source: "bg-purple-500/20 text-purple-400",
  }

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-[#0a0a0f] text-white">
      <div className="max-w-5xl mx-auto px-6 py-16">
        {/* Breadcrumb */}
        <nav className="text-sm text-gray-500 mb-8">
          <Link href="/" className="hover:text-white">Home</Link>
          {" / "}
          <Link href="/use-cases" className="hover:text-white">Use Cases</Link>
          {" / "}
          <span className="text-gray-300">{uc.name}</span>
        </nav>

        {/* Header */}
        <div className="mb-12">
          <div className="text-5xl mb-4">{uc.icon}</div>
          <h1 className="text-4xl md:text-5xl font-bold mb-4">{uc.name}</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xl">{uc.description}</p>
        </div>

        {/* Workflow if available */}
        {workflow && (
          <section className="mb-12">
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6 text-indigo-400">
              📋 Recommended Pipeline
            </h2>
            <div className="relative">
              <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
                {workflow.steps.map((step, i) => {
                  const stepTool = toolsBySlug[step.tool_slug]
                  return (
                    <div key={i} className="flex items-start gap-4">
                      <div className="flex flex-col items-center">
                        <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-indigo-500/20 border border-indigo-500/40 flex items-center justify-center text-indigo-400 font-bold text-sm flex-shrink-0">
                          {i + 1}
                        </div>
                        {i < workflow.steps.length - 1 && (
                          <div className="w-px h-8 bg-indigo-500/20 mt-1" />
                        )}
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex-1 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl p-4 mb-0">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-1">
                          <span className="font-bold text-white">
                            {stepTool?.name ?? step.tool_name ?? step.tool_slug}
                          </span>
                          {stepTool && (
                            <Link
                              href={`/tool/${step.tool_slug}`}
                              className="text-xs text-indigo-400 hover:underline"
                            >
                              View tool →
                            </Link>
                          )}
                        </div>
                        <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">{step.description}</p>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  )
                })}
              </div>
            </div>
          </section>
        )}

        {/* Tools */}
        <section>
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">
            🛠️ Best Tools for This Use Case
          </h2>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            {ucTools.map((tool) => (
              <Link
                key={tool.slug}

                className="group bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/10 hover:border-indigo-500/40 rounded-xl p-5 transition-all"
              >
                <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-2">

                    {tool.name}
                  </h3>

                    className={`text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded-full ${
                      PRICING_COLOR[tool.pricing.toLowerCase()] ?? "bg-white/10 text-gray-400"
                    }`}
                  >
                    {tool.pricing}
                  </span>
                </div>
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm line-clamp-2">{tool.description}</p>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1 mt-3">
                  <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★</span>
                  <span className="text-sm text-gray-300">{tool.rating.toFixed(1)}</span>
                  <span className="text-gray-600 text-xs ml-2">{tool.category}</span>
                </div>
              </Link>
            ))}
          </div>
        </section>
      </div>
    </main>
  )
}

import { getWorkflows, getTools } from "@/lib/db"
import { notFound } from "next/navigation"
import Link from "next/link"

export const revalidate = 86400

export async function generateStaticParams() {
  const workflows = getWorkflows()
  return workflows.map((w) => ({ slug: w.slug }))
}

export default function WorkflowDetailPage({ params }: { params: { slug: string } }) {
  const workflows = getWorkflows()
  const workflow = workflows.find((w) => w.slug === params.slug)
  if (!workflow) notFound()

  const tools = getTools()
  const toolsBySlug = Object.fromEntries(tools.map((t) => [t.slug, t]))

  const CATEGORY_EMOJI: Record<string, string> = {
    video: "🎬", writing: "✍️", audio: "🎵", code_assistant: "💻",
    marketing: "📣", research: "🔬", productivity: "⚙️",
    image_generation: "🎨", llm: "🧠", design: "🎨",
  }

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-[#0a0a0f] text-white">
      <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-6 py-12">
        <nav className="text-sm text-gray-500 mb-8">
          <Link href="/" className="hover:text-white">Home</Link>
          {" / "}
          <Link href="/workflows" className="hover:text-white">Workflows</Link>
          {" / "}
          <span className="text-gray-300">{workflow.name}</span>
        </nav>

        <div className="mb-10">
          <div className="text-5xl mb-4">
            {CATEGORY_EMOJI[workflow.category ?? ""] ?? "🔗"}
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-4xl font-bold mb-3">{workflow.name}</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-lg mb-3">{workflow.description}</p>
          {workflow.use_case && (
            <span className="text-sm bg-indigo-500/20 text-indigo-400 border border-indigo-500/30 px-3 py-1 rounded-full">
              {workflow.use_case}
            </span>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Pipeline visualization */}
        <section className="mb-12">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-8">Pipeline Steps</h2>
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {workflow.steps
              .sort((a, b) => a.step_order - b.step_order)
              .map((step, i) => {
                const tool = toolsBySlug[step.tool_slug]
                const isLast = i === workflow.steps.length - 1
                return (
                  <div key={i}>
                    <div className="flex items-start gap-4 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 hover:border-indigo-500/30 rounded-2xl p-5 transition-all">
                      <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-indigo-500/20 border border-indigo-500/30 flex items-center justify-center text-indigo-400 font-bold text-sm flex-shrink-0">
                        {step.step_order}
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex-1">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-1">
                          <span className="font-bold text-white text-lg">
                            {tool?.name ?? step.tool_name ?? step.tool_slug}
                          </span>
                          {tool && (
                            <Link
                              href={`/tool/${step.tool_slug}`}
                              className="text-xs bg-indigo-500/20 text-indigo-400 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full hover:bg-indigo-500/30 transition-colors"
                            >
                              View Tool →
                            </Link>
                          )}
                        </div>
                        <p className="text-gray-400">{step.description}</p>
                        {tool && (
                          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-2 text-xs text-gray-500">
                            <span className="capitalize">{tool.category.replace(/_/g, " ")}</span>
                            <span>•</span>
                            <span className="capitalize">{tool.pricing}</span>
                            <span>•</span>
                            <span>⭐ {tool.rating.toFixed(1)}</span>
                          </div>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    {!isLast && (
                      <div className="flex justify-center my-1">
                        <div className="text-indigo-500/50 text-2xl">↓</div>
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                )
              })}
          </div>
        </section>

        {/* Tools summary */}
        <section>
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">Tools in This Workflow</h2>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
            {workflow.steps.map((step) => {
              const tool = toolsBySlug[step.tool_slug]
              if (!tool) return null
              return (
                <Link
                  key={step.tool_slug}
                  href={`/tool/${step.tool_slug}`}
                  className="bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/10 hover:border-indigo-500/30 rounded-xl p-4 transition-all group"
                >
                  <div className="font-medium text-white group-hover:text-indigo-400 transition-colors mb-1">
                    {tool.name}
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-gray-500 capitalize">
                    {tool.pricing} • ⭐ {tool.rating.toFixed(1)}
                  </div>
                </Link>
              )
            })}
          </div>
        </section>
      </div>
    </main>
  )
}

import { getCompanies, getTools, type Company, type Tool } from "@/lib/db"

export type { Company } from "@/lib/db"

export function getAllCompanies(): Company[] {
  return getCompanies()
}

export function getCompanyBySlug(slug: string): Company | undefined {
  return getCompanies().find((c) => c.slug === slug)
}

export function getCompanyTools(companySlug: string): Tool[] {
  return getTools().filter((t) => t.company_slug === companySlug)
}

export function getTopCompanies(limit: number = 20): Company[] {
  return getCompanies()
    .sort((a, b) => b.tools.length - a.tools.length)
    .slice(0, limit)
}

export function getCompaniesByCountry(): { country: string; count: number }[] {
  const companies = getCompanies()
  const map = new Map<string, number>()
  
  for (const c of companies) {
    const country = c.hq_country || "Unknown"
    map.set(country, (map.get(country) || 0) + 1)
  }
  
  return Array.from(map.entries())
    .map(([country, count]) => ({ country, count }))
    .sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count)
}

import { getAllTools, type Tool } from "@/atlas/tools"

export function getToolsForComparison(slugs: string[]): Tool[] {
  const tools = getAllTools()
  const limited = slugs.slice(0, 4)
  return limited
    .map((slug) => tools.find((t) => t.slug === slug))
    .filter((t): t is Tool => t !== undefined)
}

export interface ComparisonField {
  key: keyof Tool | string
  label: string
}

export function getComparisonFields(): ComparisonField[] {
  return [
    { key: "name", label: "Name" },
    { key: "description", label: "Description" },
    { key: "website", label: "Website" },
    { key: "category", label: "Category" },
    { key: "pricing", label: "Pricing" },
    { key: "rating", label: "Rating" },
    { key: "company", label: "Company" },
    { key: "features", label: "Features" },
    { key: "tags", label: "Tags" },
  ]
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./atlas/graph.ts
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

import { getTools, getCompanies, type Tool } from "@/lib/db"

interface GraphNode {
  id: string
  label: string
  type: "tool" | "category" | "company" | "tag"
  size?: number
}

interface GraphEdge {
  source: string
  target: string
  type: string
}

export interface GraphData {
  nodes: GraphNode[]
  edges: GraphEdge[]
}

export function getGraphData(): GraphData {
  const tools = getTools()
  const companies = getCompanies()
  const nodes: GraphNode[] = []
  const edges: GraphEdge[] = []
  const nodeIds = new Set<string>()

  // Add category nodes
  const categoryMap = new Map<string, number>()
  for (const tool of tools) {
    categoryMap.set(tool.category, (categoryMap.get(tool.category) || 0) + 1)
  }
  
  for (const [cat, count] of categoryMap.entries()) {
    const id = `cat-${cat}`
    if (!nodeIds.has(id)) {
      nodes.push({ id, label: cat.replace(/_/g, " "), type: "category", size: Math.min(count * 2, 40) })
      nodeIds.add(id)
    }
  }

  // Add company nodes (top 50)
  const topCompanies = companies.slice(0, 50)
  for (const company of topCompanies) {
    const id = `company-${company.slug}`
    if (!nodeIds.has(id)) {
      nodes.push({ id, label: company.name, type: "company", size: Math.min(company.tools.length * 3, 30) })
      nodeIds.add(id)
    }
  }

  // Add tool nodes (limit to top 100 by rating for readability)
  const topTools = [...tools].sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating).slice(0, 100)
  
  for (const tool of topTools) {
    const toolId = `tool-${tool.slug}`
    if (!nodeIds.has(toolId)) {
      nodes.push({ id: toolId, label: tool.name, type: "tool", size: 8 })
      nodeIds.add(toolId)
    }

    // Tool -> Category edge
    const catId = `cat-${tool.category}`
    if (nodeIds.has(catId)) {
      edges.push({ source: toolId, target: catId, type: "tool_category" })
    }

    // Tool -> Company edge
    if (tool.company_slug) {
      const companyId = `company-${tool.company_slug}`
      if (nodeIds.has(companyId)) {
        edges.push({ source: toolId, target: companyId, type: "tool_company" })
      }
    }
  }

  return { nodes, edges }
}

interface ScoredTool {

  score: number
}

const SEMANTIC_MAP: Record<string, string[]> = {

  agents: ["chatgpt", "claude", "langchain", "llamaindex"],
  automation: ["zapier-ai", "make", "bardeen", "langchain"],
  avatar: ["heygen", "synthesia", "d-id"],
  upscale: ["topaz-video-ai", "magnific-ai"],
  "youtube video": ["chatgpt", "midjourney", "runway-ml", "elevenlabs", "opus-clip"],
  "faceless youtube": ["chatgpt", "elevenlabs", "pika", "suno", "midjourney"],
  "blog post": ["chatgpt", "perplexity", "grammarly", "surfer-seo", "midjourney"],
  "marketing campaign": ["chatgpt", "midjourney", "adcreative-ai", "predis-ai"],
  podcast: ["elevenlabs", "descript", "assemblyai", "notion-ai"],
  "web app": ["cursor", "v0-by-vercel", "github-copilot", "bolt-new"],
  "research paper": ["elicit", "semantic-scholar", "chatpdf", "claude"],
}

// Natural language problem → capability mapping
const PROBLEM_TO_CAPABILITY: Record<string, string[]> = {
  "write": ["text-generation"],
  "create text": ["text-generation"],
  "generate image": ["image-generation"],
  "create image": ["image-generation"],
  "make video": ["video-generation"],
  "create video": ["video-generation"],
  "generate voice": ["voice-speech"],
  "clone voice": ["voice-speech"],
  "text to speech": ["voice-speech"],
  "make music": ["music-generation"],
  "compose music": ["music-generation"],
  "write code": ["code-generation"],
  "build app": ["code-generation"],
  "analyze data": ["data-analysis"],
  "research": ["search-research"],
  "automate": ["automation"],
  "chatbot": ["chatbot-agents"],
  "translate": ["translation"],
  "transcribe": ["meeting-transcription"],
  "meeting notes": ["meeting-transcription"],
  "presentation": ["presentation"],
  "design": ["design-creative"],
  "marketing": ["seo-marketing"],
  "seo": ["seo-marketing"],
  "3d model": ["3d-spatial"],
}

// ============================================================
// Main Search Function
// Multi-signal scoring: name, tags, category, description,
// semantic map, capabilities, and rating boost
// ============================================================

export function searchTools(query: string, limit = 50): Tool[] {
  const q = query.trim().toLowerCase()
  if (!q) return []

  const terms = q.split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean)
  const tools = getTools()

  // Check semantic map for direct slug boosts
  const semanticSlugs = new Set<string>()
  for (const [keyword, slugs] of Object.entries(SEMANTIC_MAP)) {
    if (q.includes(keyword)) {
      slugs.forEach((s) => semanticSlugs.add(s))
    }
  }

  // Check problem-to-capability mapping
  const matchedCapabilities = new Set<string>()
  for (const [problem, caps] of Object.entries(PROBLEM_TO_CAPABILITY)) {
    if (q.includes(problem)) {
      caps.forEach((c) => matchedCapabilities.add(c))
    }
  }

  const scored: ScoredTool[] = tools.map((tool) => {
    let score = 0
    const nameLower = tool.name.toLowerCase()
    const descLower = tool.description.toLowerCase()
    const slugLower = tool.slug.toLowerCase()

    // Semantic boost (highest priority — direct match to known tools)
    if (semanticSlugs.has(tool.slug)) score += 15

    // Capability match boost
    if (matchedCapabilities.size > 0 && tool.capabilities?.length) {
      const capMatch = tool.capabilities.filter((c) => matchedCapabilities.has(c))
      score += capMatch.length * 6
    }

    for (const term of terms) {
      // Exact name match (strongest signal)
      if (nameLower === term) score += 25
      // Name starts with term
      else if (nameLower.startsWith(term)) score += 10
      // Name contains term
      else if (nameLower.includes(term)) score += 6

      // Slug match
      if (slugLower.includes(term)) score += 4

      // Tag exact match
      if (tool.tags?.some((tag) => tag.toLowerCase() === term)) score += 5
      // Tag partial match
      else if (tool.tags?.some((tag) => tag.toLowerCase().includes(term))) score += 2.5

      // Capability slug match
      if (tool.capabilities?.some((cap) => cap.includes(term))) score += 4

      // Company match
      if (tool.company?.toLowerCase().includes(term)) score += 2

      // Category match
      if (tool.category.toLowerCase().includes(term)) score += 3
      if (tool.category.replace(/_/g, " ").toLowerCase().includes(term)) score += 2

      // Description match
      if (descLower.includes(term)) score += 1.5

      // Feature match
      if (tool.features?.some((f) => f.toLowerCase().includes(term))) score += 1

      // Long description match
      if (tool.long_description?.toLowerCase().includes(term)) score += 0.5

      // Platform match
      if (tool.platforms?.some((p) => p.toLowerCase().includes(term))) score += 1
    }

    // Bonus: open source query
    if (q.includes("open source") && tool.is_open_source) score += 8
    if (q.includes("free") && (tool.pricing === "free" || tool.pricing_details?.free_tier)) score += 6
    if (q.includes("api") && tool.has_api) score += 5

    // Rating boost (small, but breaks ties)
    score += tool.rating * 0.15

    return { tool, score }
  })

  return scored
    .filter((s) => s.score > 0)
    .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)
    .slice(0, limit)
    .map((s) => s.tool)
}

// ============================================================
// Search by Use Case
// ============================================================

export function searchByUseCase(query: string): UseCase[] {
  const q = query.trim().toLowerCase()
  if (!q) return []
  const terms = q.split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean)
  const useCases = getUseCases()

  return useCases
    .map((uc) => {
      let score = 0
      const nameLower = uc.name.toLowerCase()
      const descLower = uc.description.toLowerCase()

      for (const term of terms) {
        if (nameLower.includes(term)) score += 5
        if (descLower.includes(term)) score += 2
        if (uc.slug.includes(term)) score += 3
      }
      return { uc, score }
    })
    .filter((s) => s.score > 0)
    .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)
    .map((s) => s.uc)
}

// ============================================================
// Get tools for a specific use case
// ============================================================

export function getToolsForUseCase(slug: string): Tool[] {
  const useCases = getUseCases()
  const uc = useCases.find((u) => u.slug === slug)
  if (!uc) return []
  const tools = getTools()
  return uc.tool_slugs
    .map((s) => tools.find((t) => t.slug === s))
    .filter((t): t is Tool => !!t)
}

// ============================================================
// Alternatives System
// Finds similar tools based on category, tags, capabilities,
// pricing, and rating
// ============================================================

export function getAlternatives(tool: Tool, limit = 6): Tool[] {
  const tools = getTools()
  const scored = tools
    .filter((t) => t.slug !== tool.slug)
    .map((t) => {
      let score = 0

      // Same category (strongest signal)
      if (t.category === tool.category) score += 8

      // Shared tags
      const sharedTags = t.tags?.filter((tag) => tool.tags?.includes(tag)) ?? []
      score += sharedTags.length * 2

      // Shared capabilities
      const sharedCaps = t.capabilities?.filter((c) => tool.capabilities?.includes(c)) ?? []
      score += sharedCaps.length * 3

      // Same pricing model
      if (t.pricing === tool.pricing) score += 1

      // Rating boost
      score += t.rating * 0.3

      return { tool: t, score }
    })
    .filter((s) => s.score > 3)
    .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)
    .slice(0, limit)

  return scored.map((s) => s.tool)
}

// ============================================================
// Trending Tools
// Returns top-rated tools across diverse categories
// In production, this would use actual analytics data
// ============================================================

export function getTrendingTools(limit = 12): Tool[] {
  const tools = getTools()
  const categoryMap = new Map<string, Tool[]>()

  for (const tool of tools) {
    if (!categoryMap.has(tool.category)) categoryMap.set(tool.category, [])
    categoryMap.get(tool.category)!.push(tool)
  }

  const trending: Tool[] = []
  // Get top 2 from each category for diversity
  for (const catTools of categoryMap.values()) {
    const sorted = catTools.sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating)
    trending.push(...sorted.slice(0, 2))
  }

  return trending
    .sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating)
    .slice(0, limit)
}

// ============================================================
// Capability-based Tool Discovery
// ============================================================

export function getToolsForCapability(capSlug: string, limit = 20): Tool[] {
  return getToolsByCapability(capSlug)
    .sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating)
    .slice(0, limit)
}

export function getCapabilityStats(): { capability: Capability; toolCount: number }[] {
  const capabilities = getCapabilities()
  const tools = getTools()

  return capabilities.map((cap) => ({
    capability: cap,
    toolCount: tools.filter((t) => t.capabilities?.includes(cap.slug)).length,
  })).sort((a, b) => b.toolCount - a.toolCount)
}

// ============================================================
// Smart Search — combines tools + use cases + capabilities
// Returns a unified result for the search page
// ============================================================

export interface SmartSearchResult {
  tools: Tool[]
  useCases: UseCase[]
  matchedCapabilities: Capability[]
}

export function smartSearch(query: string): SmartSearchResult {
  const tools = searchTools(query, 30)
  const useCases = searchByUseCase(query)

  const q = query.trim().toLowerCase()
  const capabilities = getCapabilities()
  const matchedCapabilities = capabilities.filter(
    (cap) =>
      cap.name.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      cap.slug.includes(q.replace(/\s+/g, "-")) ||
      cap.description.toLowerCase().includes(q)
  )

  return { tools, useCases, matchedCapabilities }
}
