import { getTools, getCompanies, type Tool, type Company } from "@/lib/db"

export type { Tool, Company } from "@/lib/db"

export function getAllTools(): Tool[] {
  return getTools()
}

export function getToolBySlug(slug: string): Tool | undefined {
  return getTools().find((t) => t.slug === slug)
}

export function getToolsByCategory(category: string): Tool[] {
  return getTools().filter(
    (t) => t.category.toLowerCase() === category.toLowerCase()
  )
}

const CATEGORY_ICONS: Record<string, string> = {
  "ai": "🤖", "analytics": "📊", "api": "🔌", "automation": "⚡",
  "audio": "🎵", "backend": "🖥️", "ci/cd": "🔄", "cloud": "☁️",
  "cloud_ai": "☁️", "cms": "📝", "code_assistant": "💻",
  "collaboration": "🤝", "communication": "💬", "crm": "👥",
  "data": "🗄️", "database": "💾", "design": "🎨", "deployment": "🚀",
  "devops": "🔧", "documentation": "📄", "ecommerce": "🛒",
  "editor": "✏️", "education": "📚", "email": "📧", "finance": "💰",
  "frontend": "🖼️", "healthcare": "🏥", "hosting": "🏠", "ide": "💻",
  "image_generation": "🎨", "infrastructure": "🏗️", "llm": "🧠",
  "logging": "📋", "marketing": "📣", "mobile": "📱", "monitoring": "👁️",
  "networking": "🌐", "no-code": "🧩", "observability": "🔭",
  "orm": "🔗", "payment": "💳", "productivity": "⚙️",
  "project management": "📅", "research": "🔬", "robotics": "🤖",
  "saas": "☁️", "search": "🔍", "security": "🔒", "storage": "📦",
  "testing": "🧪", "version control": "📚", "video": "🎬",
  "writing": "✍️",
}

function getIconForCategory(name: string): string {
  const lower = name.toLowerCase()
  for (const [key, icon] of Object.entries(CATEGORY_ICONS)) {
    if (lower.includes(key)) return icon
  }
  return "🔹"
}

function toSlug(name: string): string {
  return name.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, "-").replace(/(^-|-$)/g, "")
}

export function getCategories(): { name: string; slug: string; count: number; icon: string }[] {
  const tools = getTools()
  const map = new Map<string, number>()

  for (const tool of tools) {
    map.set(tool.category, (map.get(tool.category) || 0) + 1)
  }

  return Array.from(map.entries())
    .map(([name, count]) => ({
      name,
      slug: toSlug(name),
      count,
      icon: getIconForCategory(name),
    }))
    .sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count)
}

export function getFeaturedTools(limit: number = 12): Tool[] {
  const tools = getTools()
  return [...tools].sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating).slice(0, limit)
}

export function getRecentTools(limit: number = 8): Tool[] {
  const tools = getTools()
  return tools.slice(-limit).reverse()
}

export function getRelatedTools(tool: Tool, limit: number = 6): Tool[] {
  return getTools()
    .filter((t) => t.category === tool.category && t.slug !== tool.slug)
    .sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating)
    .slice(0, limit)
}

export function getTopRatedTools(limit: number = 10): Tool[] {
  return [...getTools()].sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating).slice(0, limit)
}

export function getToolStats() {
  const tools = getTools()
  const companies = getCompanies()
  const categories = getCategories()
  const avgRating = tools.reduce((sum, t) => sum + t.rating, 0) / tools.length
  
  return {
    totalTools: tools.length,
    totalCompanies: companies.length,
    totalCategories: categories.length,
    avgRating: Math.round(avgRating * 10) / 10,
    freeTools: tools.filter(t => t.pricing.toLowerCase() === "free" || t.pricing.toLowerCase() === "open_source").length,
  }
}

import { getWorkflows, getTools, type Workflow, type Tool } from "@/lib/db"

export type { Workflow, WorkflowStep } from "@/lib/db"

export function getAllWorkflows(): Workflow[] {
  return getWorkflows()
}

export function getWorkflowBySlug(slug: string): Workflow | undefined {
  return getWorkflows().find((w) => w.slug === slug)
}

export function getWorkflowWithTools(slug: string): (Workflow & { toolDetails: (Tool | null)[] }) | undefined {
  const workflow = getWorkflowBySlug(slug)
  if (!workflow) return undefined
  
  const tools = getTools()
  const toolDetails = workflow.steps.map(step => 
    tools.find(t => t.slug === step.tool_slug) || null
  )
  
  return { ...workflow, toolDetails }
}

export function getWorkflowsByUseCase(useCase: string): Workflow[] {
  return getWorkflows().filter(w => 
    w.use_case.toLowerCase() === useCase.toLowerCase()
  )
}

export function getUseCases(): { name: string; count: number }[] {
  const workflows = getWorkflows()
  const map = new Map<string, number>()
  
  for (const w of workflows) {
    map.set(w.use_case, (map.get(w.use_case) || 0) + 1)
  }
  
  return Array.from(map.entries())
    .map(([name, count]) => ({ name, count }))
    .sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count)
}

          </span>

"use client";

import { ExternalLink } from "lucide-react";

interface Tool {
  name: string;
  slug: string;
  description: string;
  website: string;
  category: string;
  pricing: string;
  company: string;
  tags: string[];
}

const pricingColors: Record<string, string> = {
  Free: "bg-teal/20 text-teal-light",
  Freemium: "bg-gold/20 text-gold-light",
  Paid: "bg-rust/20 text-rust",
  "Open Source": "bg-teal/20 text-teal-light",
  "Free Trial": "bg-gold/20 text-gold-light",
};

export default function CompareTable({ tools }: { tools: Tool[] }) {
  if (!tools || tools.length === 0) {
    return (
      <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-20 gap-4">
        <p className="text-mist/60 font-mono text-sm">No tools selected for comparison.</p>
        <p className="text-mist/40 font-mono text-xs">Add tools using the search above.</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const rows: { label: string; render: (tool: Tool) => React.ReactNode }[] = [
    {
      label: "Description",
      render: (t) => <span className="text-sm text-mist leading-relaxed">{t.description}</span>,
    },
    {
      label: "Website",
      render: (t) =>
        t.website ? (
          <a
            href={t.website}
            target="_blank"
            rel="noopener noreferrer"
            className="text-sm text-teal-light hover:text-teal underline inline-flex items-center gap-1"
          >
            Visit <ExternalLink size={12} />
          </a>
        ) : (
          <span className="text-mist/40 text-sm">—</span>
        ),
    },
    {
      label: "Category",
      render: (t) => (
        <span className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-mist">
          {t.category.replace(/-/g, " ")}
        </span>
      ),
    },
    {
      label: "Pricing",
      render: (t) => {
        const colorClass = pricingColors[t.pricing] || "bg-mist/20 text-mist";
        return (
          <span className={`inline-block text-[10px] font-mono uppercase tracking-wider px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${colorClass}`}>
            {t.pricing}
          </span>
        );
      },
    },
    {
      label: "Company",
      render: (t) => <span className="text-sm text-paper">{t.company}</span>,
    },
    {
      label: "Tags",
      render: (t) => (
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
          {(t.tags || []).slice(0, 6).map((tag) => (
            <span
              key={tag}
              className="text-[10px] font-mono px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-gold/10 text-mist/80"
            >
              {tag}
            </span>
          ))}
        </div>
      ),
    },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="overflow-x-auto rounded-xl border border-gold/10">
      <table className="w-full min-w-[640px]">
        {/* Header */}
        <thead>
          <tr className="border-b border-gold/10">
            <th className="text-left p-4 w-32">
              <span className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-widest text-mist/40">Field</span>
            </th>
            {tools.map((tool) => (
              <th key={tool.slug} className="p-4 text-center">
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-2">
                  <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-full bg-gold/10 flex items-center justify-center font-display text-xl text-gold">
                    {tool.name.charAt(0)}
                  </div>
                  <span className="font-semibold text-paper text-sm">{tool.name}</span>
                </div>
              </th>
            ))}
          </tr>
        </thead>

        {/* Body */}
        <tbody>
          {rows.map((row, idx) => (
            <tr
              key={row.label}
              className={`border-b border-gold/5 ${idx % 2 === 0 ? "bg-surface" : "bg-ink"}`}
            >
              <td className="p-4 align-top">
                <span className="font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-mist/50">
                  {row.label}
                </span>
              </td>
              {tools.map((tool) => (
                <td key={tool.slug} className="p-4 align-top text-center">
                  {row.render(tool)}
                </td>
              ))}
            </tr>
          ))}
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  );
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗

"use client";

import { Check, X } from "lucide-react";

interface Tool {
  name: string;
  features: string[];
}

export default function FeatureMatrix({ tools }: { tools: Tool[] }) {
  if (!tools || tools.length === 0) return null;

  // Collect all unique features
  const allFeatures = Array.from(
    new Set(tools.flatMap((t) => t.features || []))
  ).sort();

  if (allFeatures.length === 0) return null;

  return (
    <div className="overflow-x-auto rounded-sm border border-gold/10">
      <table className="w-full">
        <thead>
          <tr className="border-b border-gold/10">
            <th className="text-left p-4 font-mono text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-mist/60 bg-surface sticky left-0">
              Feature
            </th>
            {tools.map((tool) => (
              <th
                key={tool.name}
                className="p-4 font-display text-sm text-paper text-center min-w-[140px] bg-surface"
              >
                {tool.name}
              </th>
            ))}
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          {allFeatures.map((feature, i) => (
            <tr
              key={feature}
              className={`border-b border-paper/5 ${i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-ink" : "bg-surface/50"}`}
            >
              <td className="p-4 text-sm text-mist font-mono sticky left-0 bg-inherit">
                {feature}
              </td>
              {tools.map((tool) => {
                const has = tool.features?.includes(feature);
                return (
                  <td key={tool.name} className="p-4 text-center">
                    {has ? (
                      <Check size={16} className="text-teal-light mx-auto" />
                    ) : (
                      <X size={16} className="text-mist/20 mx-auto" />
                    )}
                  </td>
                );
              })}
            </tr>
          ))}
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  );
}

"use client";

import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";

interface Company {
  name: string;
  lat: number;
  lng: number;
}

const companies: Company[] = [
  { name: "OpenAI", lat: 37.77, lng: -122.41 },
  { name: "Anthropic", lat: 37.77, lng: -122.42 },
  { name: "Google DeepMind", lat: 51.50, lng: -0.12 },
  { name: "Mistral", lat: 48.85, lng: 2.35 },
  { name: "Stability AI", lat: 51.51, lng: -0.13 },
  { name: "Meta AI", lat: 37.48, lng: -122.15 },
  { name: "DeepSeek", lat: 30.27, lng: 120.15 },
  { name: "Hugging Face", lat: 40.71, lng: -74.00 },
  { name: "Samsung", lat: 37.56, lng: 126.97 },
  { name: "Baidu", lat: 39.90, lng: 116.40 },
  { name: "Alibaba", lat: 30.27, lng: 120.19 },
  { name: "NVIDIA", lat: 37.37, lng: -121.96 },
  { name: "Adobe", lat: 37.33, lng: -121.89 },
  { name: "Cohere", lat: 43.65, lng: -79.38 },
  { name: "xAI", lat: 78.23, lng: 15.63 },
  { name: "Apple", lat: 37.33, lng: -122.01 },
];

const arcs = [
  { start: 0, end: 2 }, { start: 0, end: 3 }, { start: 0, end: 5 },
  { start: 0, end: 6 }, { start: 2, end: 3 }, { start: 2, end: 4 },
  { start: 5, end: 11 }, { start: 7, end: 3 }, { start: 8, end: 9 },
  { start: 9, end: 10 }, { start: 1, end: 7 }, { start: 0, end: 14 },
];

type Layer = "companies" | "network" | "funding" | "activity";

interface GlobeVisualizationProps {
  height?: string;
}

export default function GlobeVisualization({ height = "h-[600px]" }: GlobeVisualizationProps) {
  const globeRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const globeInstanceRef = useRef<any>(null);
  const [activeLayer, setActiveLayer] = useState<Layer>("companies");
  const [loaded, setLoaded] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    let cancelled = false;

    const loadScript = (src: string): Promise<void> =>
      new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        if (document.querySelector(`script[src="${src}"]`)) {
          resolve();
          return;
        }
        const script = document.createElement("script");
        script.src = src;
        script.onload = () => resolve();
        script.onerror = reject;
        document.head.appendChild(script);
      });

    const init = async () => {
      try {
        await loadScript("https://unpkg.com/three@0.160.0/build/three.min.js");
        await loadScript("https://unpkg.com/globe.gl@2.33.0/dist/globe.gl.min.js");

        if (cancelled || !globeRef.current) return;

        const Globe = (window as any).Globe;
        if (!Globe) return;

        const globe = Globe()(globeRef.current)
          .globeImageUrl("//unpkg.com/three-globe/example/img/earth-dark.jpg")
          .backgroundColor("#07090f")
          .atmosphereColor("#1a7a6e")
          .atmosphereAltitude(0.2)
          .pointsData(companies)
          .pointLat("lat")
          .pointLng("lng")
          .pointColor(() => "#c9a84c")
          .pointAltitude(0.06)
          .pointRadius(0.5)
          .pointLabel((d: any) => `<div style="color:#f5f0e8;font-family:monospace;font-size:12px;background:#0a0a0f;padding:4px 8px;border:1px solid #c9a84c33;border-radius:6px">${d.name}</div>`)
          .arcsData(
            arcs.map((a) => ({
              startLat: companies[a.start].lat,
              startLng: companies[a.start].lng,
              endLat: companies[a.end].lat,
              endLng: companies[a.end].lng,
            }))
          )
          .arcColor(() => ["#1a7a6e88", "#c9a84c88"])
          .arcStroke(0.4)
          .arcDashLength(0.6)
          .arcDashGap(0.3)
          .arcDashAnimateTime(3000)
          .enablePointerInteraction(true);

        globe.controls().autoRotate = true;
        globe.controls().autoRotateSpeed = 0.5;

        globeInstanceRef.current = globe;
        setLoaded(true);

        const handleResize = () => {
          if (globeRef.current && globeInstanceRef.current) {
            globeInstanceRef.current.width(globeRef.current.clientWidth);
            globeInstanceRef.current.height(globeRef.current.clientHeight);
          }
        };
        window.addEventListener("resize", handleResize);
        handleResize();

        return () => window.removeEventListener("resize", handleResize);
      } catch (err) {
        console.error("Globe loading failed:", err);
      }
    };

    init();

    return () => {
      cancelled = true;
      if (globeInstanceRef.current) {
        globeInstanceRef.current._destructor?.();
      }
    };
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    const globe = globeInstanceRef.current;
    if (!globe || !loaded) return;

    switch (activeLayer) {
      case "companies":
        globe
          .pointsData(companies)
          .pointColor(() => "#c9a84c")
          .pointAltitude(0.06)
          .arcsData(
            arcs.map((a) => ({
              startLat: companies[a.start].lat,
              startLng: companies[a.start].lng,
              endLat: companies[a.end].lat,
              endLng: companies[a.end].lng,
            }))
          )
          .arcStroke(0.4)
          .heatmapsData([]);
        break;
      case "network":
        globe
          .arcStroke(1)
          .arcColor(() => ["#2ab8a5", "#c9a84c"])
          .pointAltitude(0.03);
        break;
      case "funding":
        globe
          .pointColor(() => "#c9a84c")
          .pointAltitude((d: any) => {
            const idx = companies.findIndex((c) => c.name === d.name);
            return [0.15, 0.12, 0.1, 0.08, 0.07, 0.09, 0.06, 0.05, 0.08, 0.07, 0.1, 0.11, 0.09, 0.04, 0.06, 0.13][idx] || 0.05;
          })
          .pointRadius(0.8);
        break;
      case "activity":
        globe
          .pointColor(() => "#c45c2a")
          .pointRadius(1.2)
          .pointAltitude(0.02);
        break;
    }
  }, [activeLayer, loaded]);

  const layers: { key: Layer; label: string }[] = [
    { key: "companies", label: "Companies" },
    { key: "network", label: "Network" },
    { key: "funding", label: "Funding" },
    { key: "activity", label: "AI Activity" },
  ];

  return (
    <div className={`relative ${height} w-full rounded-xl overflow-hidden bg-[#07090f]`}>
      {/* Panel overlay */}
      <div className="absolute top-4 left-4 z-10 flex flex-col gap-3">
        <h3 className="font-display text-lg text-paper">AI Globe</h3>
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-1.5">
          {layers.map((layer) => (
            <button
              key={layer.key}
              onClick={() => setActiveLayer(layer.key)}
              className={`text-left font-mono text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg border transition-all ${
                activeLayer === layer.key
                  ? "bg-gold/20 border-gold/40 text-gold"
                  : "bg-ink/60 border-gold/10 text-mist hover:text-paper hover:border-gold/20"
              }`}
            >
              {layer.label}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Globe container */}
      <div ref={globeRef} className="w-full h-full" />

      {!loaded && (
        <div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center">
          <span className="font-mono text-sm text-mist/50 animate-pulse">Loading globe...</span>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./components/KnowledgeGraph.tsx
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

"use client";

import { useEffect, useRef, useState, useCallback } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";

interface GraphNode {
  id: string;
  label: string;
  type: "tool" | "category" | "company";
  slug?: string;
  x: number;
  y: number;
  vx: number;
  vy: number;
}

interface GraphLink {
  source: string;
  target: string;
}

interface GraphData {
  nodes: { id: string; label: string; type: string; slug?: string }[];
  links: { source: string; target: string }[];
}

const NODE_COLORS: Record<string, string> = {
  tool: "#1a7a6e",
  category: "#c9a84c",
  company: "#c45c2a",
};

const NODE_RADIUS: Record<string, number> = {
  tool: 6,
  category: 10,
  company: 8,
};

export default function KnowledgeGraph() {
  const canvasRef = useRef<HTMLCanvasElement>(null);
  const nodesRef = useRef<GraphNode[]>([]);
  const linksRef = useRef<GraphLink[]>([]);
  const animRef = useRef<number>(0);
  const [tooltip, setTooltip] = useState<{ x: number; y: number; node: GraphNode } | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const router = useRouter();

  // Camera state
  const cameraRef = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0, zoom: 1 });
  const dragRef = useRef<{ startX: number; startY: number; camStartX: number; camStartY: number } | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchData = async () => {
      try {
        const res = await fetch("/api/graph");
        const data: GraphData = await res.json();

        const nodes: GraphNode[] = data.nodes.map((n, i) => ({
          ...n,
          type: n.type as GraphNode["type"],
          x: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 800,
          y: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 600,
          vx: 0,
          vy: 0,
        }));

        nodesRef.current = nodes;
        linksRef.current = data.links;
        setLoading(false);
      } catch (err) {
        console.error("Failed to fetch graph data:", err);
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };

    fetchData();
  }, []);

  const screenToWorld = useCallback((sx: number, sy: number) => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return { x: 0, y: 0 };
    const cam = cameraRef.current;
    return {
      x: (sx - canvas.width / 2) / cam.zoom + cam.x,
      y: (sy - canvas.height / 2) / cam.zoom + cam.y,
    };
  }, []);

  const findNode = useCallback((wx: number, wy: number): GraphNode | null => {
    const nodes = nodesRef.current;
    for (let i = nodes.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      const n = nodes[i];
      const r = NODE_RADIUS[n.type] || 6;
      const dx = n.x - wx;
      const dy = n.y - wy;
      if (dx * dx + dy * dy < (r + 4) * (r + 4)) return n;
    }
    return null;
  }, []);

  // Force simulation
  useEffect(() => {
    if (loading) return;

    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");
    if (!ctx) return;

    const resize = () => {
      const parent = canvas.parentElement;
      if (parent) {
        canvas.width = parent.clientWidth;
        canvas.height = parent.clientHeight;
      }
    };
    resize();
    window.addEventListener("resize", resize);

    const nodeMap = new Map<string, GraphNode>();
    nodesRef.current.forEach((n) => nodeMap.set(n.id, n));

    const simulate = () => {
      const nodes = nodesRef.current;
      const links = linksRef.current;
      const damping = 0.92;
      const repulsion = 1200;
      const attraction = 0.005;
      const centerGravity = 0.01;

      // Repulsion
      for (let i = 0; i < nodes.length; i++) {
        for (let j = i + 1; j < nodes.length; j++) {
          const a = nodes[i];
          const b = nodes[j];
          let dx = a.x - b.x;
          let dy = a.y - b.y;
          let dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) || 1;
          const force = repulsion / (dist * dist);
          const fx = (dx / dist) * force;
          const fy = (dy / dist) * force;
          a.vx += fx;
          a.vy += fy;
          b.vx -= fx;
          b.vy -= fy;
        }
      }

      // Attraction
      for (const link of links) {
        const source = nodeMap.get(link.source);
        const target = nodeMap.get(link.target);
        if (!source || !target) continue;
        const dx = target.x - source.x;
        const dy = target.y - source.y;
        const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) || 1;
        const force = dist * attraction;
        const fx = (dx / dist) * force;
        const fy = (dy / dist) * force;
        source.vx += fx;
        source.vy += fy;
        target.vx -= fx;
        target.vy -= fy;
      }

      // Center gravity
      for (const node of nodes) {
        node.vx -= node.x * centerGravity;
        node.vy -= node.y * centerGravity;
        node.vx *= damping;
        node.vy *= damping;
        node.x += node.vx;
        node.y += node.vy;
      }
    };

    const draw = () => {
      const cam = cameraRef.current;
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
      ctx.fillStyle = "#07090f";
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

      ctx.save();
      ctx.translate(canvas.width / 2, canvas.height / 2);
      ctx.scale(cam.zoom, cam.zoom);
      ctx.translate(-cam.x, -cam.y);

      // Links
      ctx.strokeStyle = "rgba(138, 154, 173, 0.12)";
      ctx.lineWidth = 0.5 / cam.zoom;
      for (const link of linksRef.current) {
        const source = nodeMap.get(link.source);
        const target = nodeMap.get(link.target);
        if (!source || !target) continue;
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(source.x, source.y);
        ctx.lineTo(target.x, target.y);
        ctx.stroke();
      }

      // Nodes
      for (const node of nodesRef.current) {
        const r = NODE_RADIUS[node.type] || 6;
        const color = NODE_COLORS[node.type] || "#8a9aad";

        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(node.x, node.y, r, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = color;
        ctx.fill();

        // Label for larger nodes
        if (r >= 8 || cam.zoom > 1.5) {
          ctx.fillStyle = "#f5f0e8";
          ctx.font = `${Math.max(9, 10 / cam.zoom)}px monospace`;
          ctx.textAlign = "center";
          ctx.fillText(node.label, node.x, node.y - r - 4);
        }
      }

      ctx.restore();

      simulate();
      animRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(draw);
    };

    animRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(draw);

    return () => {
      cancelAnimationFrame(animRef.current);
      window.removeEventListener("resize", resize);
    };
  }, [loading]);

  // Mouse events
  useEffect(() => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;

    const onWheel = (e: WheelEvent) => {
      e.preventDefault();
      const cam = cameraRef.current;
      const factor = e.deltaY > 0 ? 0.9 : 1.1;
      cam.zoom = Math.max(0.1, Math.min(10, cam.zoom * factor));
    };

    const onMouseDown = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      dragRef.current = {
        startX: e.clientX,
        startY: e.clientY,
        camStartX: cameraRef.current.x,
        camStartY: cameraRef.current.y,
      };
    };

    const onMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      const sx = e.clientX - rect.left;
      const sy = e.clientY - rect.top;

      if (dragRef.current) {
        const cam = cameraRef.current;
        cam.x = dragRef.current.camStartX - (e.clientX - dragRef.current.startX) / cam.zoom;
        cam.y = dragRef.current.camStartY - (e.clientY - dragRef.current.startY) / cam.zoom;
        setTooltip(null);
        return;
      }

      const world = screenToWorld(sx, sy);
      const node = findNode(world.x, world.y);
      if (node) {
        setTooltip({ x: e.clientX - rect.left, y: e.clientY - rect.top, node });
        canvas.style.cursor = node.type === "tool" ? "pointer" : "default";
      } else {
        setTooltip(null);
        canvas.style.cursor = "grab";
      }
    };

    const onMouseUp = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (dragRef.current) {
        const dist = Math.abs(e.clientX - dragRef.current.startX) + Math.abs(e.clientY - dragRef.current.startY);
        if (dist < 5) {
          const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
          const sx = e.clientX - rect.left;
          const sy = e.clientY - rect.top;
          const world = screenToWorld(sx, sy);
          const node = findNode(world.x, world.y);
          if (node && node.type === "tool" && node.slug) {
            router.push(`/tool/${node.slug}`);
          }
        }
      }
      dragRef.current = null;
    };

    canvas.addEventListener("wheel", onWheel, { passive: false });
    canvas.addEventListener("mousedown", onMouseDown);
    canvas.addEventListener("mousemove", onMouseMove);
    canvas.addEventListener("mouseup", onMouseUp);

    return () => {
      canvas.removeEventListener("wheel", onWheel);
      canvas.removeEventListener("mousedown", onMouseDown);
      canvas.removeEventListener("mousemove", onMouseMove);
      canvas.removeEventListener("mouseup", onMouseUp);
    };
  }, [screenToWorld, findNode, router]);

  return (
    <div className="relative w-full h-full min-h-[500px]">
      <canvas ref={canvasRef} className="w-full h-full" />

      {/* Legend */}
      <div className="absolute bottom-4 left-4 bg-ink/80 backdrop-blur border border-gold/10 rounded-lg p-3 flex flex-col gap-2">
        <span className="font-mono text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest text-mist/60 mb-1">Legend</span>
        {[
          { type: "tool", label: "Tool", color: NODE_COLORS.tool },
          { type: "category", label: "Category", color: NODE_COLORS.category },
          { type: "company", label: "Company", color: NODE_COLORS.company },
        ].map((item) => (
          <div key={item.type} className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <span className="w-3 h-3 rounded-full" style={{ backgroundColor: item.color }} />
            <span className="font-mono text-xs text-mist">{item.label}</span>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Tooltip */}
      {tooltip && (
        <div
          className="absolute pointer-events-none bg-ink/90 border border-gold/20 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 backdrop-blur z-20"
          style={{ left: tooltip.x + 12, top: tooltip.y - 10 }}
        >
          <p className="font-mono text-xs text-paper">{tooltip.node.label}</p>
          <p className="font-mono text-[10px] text-mist/60 capitalize">{tooltip.node.type}</p>
        </div>
      )}

      {loading && (
        <div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center bg-ink/60">
          <span className="font-mono text-sm text-mist/50 animate-pulse">Loading graph...</span>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./components/RatingStars.tsx
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

import { Star } from "lucide-react";

export default function RatingStars({ rating, size = 14 }: { rating: number; size?: number }) {
  const full = Math.floor(rating);
  const hasHalf = rating - full >= 0.3;
  const empty = 5 - full - (hasHalf ? 1 : 0);

  return (
    <div className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
      {Array.from({ length: full }).map((_, i) => (
        <Star key={`full-${i}`} size={size} className="text-gold fill-gold" />
      ))}
      {hasHalf && (
        <div className="relative" style={{ width: size, height: size }}>
          <Star size={size} className="text-mist/20 absolute" />
          <div className="overflow-hidden absolute" style={{ width: size / 2, height: size }}>
            <Star size={size} className="text-gold fill-gold" />
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
      {Array.from({ length: empty }).map((_, i) => (
        <Star key={`empty-${i}`} size={size} className="text-mist/20" />
      ))}
      <span className="ml-1.5 font-mono text-sm text-paper">{rating.toFixed(1)}</span>
    </div>
  );
}

"use client";

import { useState, FormEvent } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { Search } from "lucide-react";

interface SearchBarProps {
  size?: "large" | "small";
  placeholder?: string;
}

export default function SearchBar({ size = "large", placeholder }: SearchBarProps) {
  const [query, setQuery] = useState("");
  const router = useRouter();

  const handleSubmit = (e: FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const trimmed = query.trim();
    if (trimmed) {
      router.push(`/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(trimmed)}`);
    }
  };

  if (size === "small") {
    return (
      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="relative w-full">
        <Search size={14} className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-mist/50" />
        <input
          type="text"
          value={query}
          onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
          placeholder={placeholder || "Search tools..."}
          className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-gold/10 rounded-lg pl-8 pr-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-mono text-paper placeholder:text-mist/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-gold/40 transition-colors"
        />
      </form>
    );
  }

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="w-full">
      <div className="flex items-center bg-white/[0.03] backdrop-blur border border-gold/30 rounded-xl overflow-hidden focus-within:border-gold/60 transition-colors">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 pl-5 pr-2 shrink-0">
          <span className="text-gold font-mono text-sm">$</span>
          <span className="text-gold/70 font-mono text-sm">find_tool</span>
        </div>
        <input
          type="text"
          value={query}
          onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
          placeholder={placeholder || "Search 503 AI tools..."}
          className="flex-1 bg-transparent py-4 px-2 text-paper font-mono text-sm placeholder:text-mist/40 focus:outline-none"
        />
        <button
          type="submit"
          className="bg-gold hover:bg-gold-light text-ink font-mono uppercase tracking-wider text-xs px-6 py-4 transition-colors shrink-0"
        >
          Search
        </button>
      </div>
    </form>
  );
}

import { LucideIcon } from "lucide-react";

interface StatsCardProps {
  label: string;
  value: string | number;
  icon: LucideIcon;
  color?: "gold" | "teal" | "rust" | "mist";
}

const colorMap = {
  gold: { bg: "bg-gold/10", text: "text-gold" },
  teal: { bg: "bg-teal/10", text: "text-teal-light" },
  rust: { bg: "bg-rust/10", text: "text-rust" },
  mist: { bg: "bg-mist/10", text: "text-mist" },
};

export default function StatsCard({ label, value, icon: Icon, color = "gold" }: StatsCardProps) {
  const colors = colorMap[color];

  return (
    <div className="bg-surface border border-gold/5 rounded-sm p-6">
      <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-4">
        <div className={`w-10 h-10 ${colors.bg} rounded-sm flex items-center justify-center`}>
          <Icon size={18} className={colors.text} />
        </div>
      </div>
      <p className="font-display text-3xl text-paper mb-1">{value}</p>
      <p className="font-mono text-xs text-mist/60 uppercase tracking-wider">{label}</p>
    </div>
  );
}

import Link from "next/link";
import { Star, ExternalLink, ArrowRight } from "lucide-react";

interface Tool {
  name: string;
  slug: string;
  description: string;
  website: string;
  category: string;
  pricing: string;
  company: string;
  tags: string[];
  logo: string | null;
  rating: number;
  features?: string[];
}

const pricingColors: Record<string, string> = {
  Free: "bg-teal/20 text-teal-light",
  Freemium: "bg-gold/20 text-gold-light",
  Paid: "bg-rust/20 text-rust",
  "Open Source": "bg-teal/20 text-teal-light",
  "Free Trial": "bg-gold/20 text-gold-light",
  free: "bg-teal/20 text-teal-light",
  freemium: "bg-gold/20 text-gold-light",
  paid: "bg-rust/20 text-rust",
  open_source: "bg-teal/20 text-teal-light",
  free_trial: "bg-gold/20 text-gold-light",
};

function formatPricing(p: string) {
  return p.replace(/_/g, " ").replace(/\b\w/g, c => c.toUpperCase());
}

export default function ToolCard({ tool }: { tool: Tool }) {
  const colorClass = pricingColors[tool.pricing] || "bg-mist/20 text-mist";

  return (
    <Link href={`/tool/${tool.slug}`} className="group block">
      <div className="bg-surface border border-gold/5 rounded-sm p-6 h-full flex flex-col transition-all duration-300 hover:border-gold/30 hover:-translate-y-1 hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-gold/5">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-4">
          <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-paper/5 border border-paper/10 rounded-sm flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
            {tool.logo ? (
              <img src={tool.logo} alt={tool.name} className="w-8 h-8 object-contain" />
            ) : (
              <span className="text-xl font-display text-gold">{tool.name.charAt(0)}</span>
            )}
          </div>
          <ArrowRight
            size={16}
            className="text-mist/0 group-hover:text-gold transition-all duration-300 group-hover:translate-x-0.5"
          />
        </div>

        {/* Name + Company */}
        <h3 className="font-display text-xl text-paper mb-1 group-hover:text-gold transition-colors">
          {tool.name}
        </h3>
        {tool.company && (
          <p className="text-mist/50 text-xs font-mono mb-3">{tool.company}</p>
        )}

        {/* Description */}
        <p className="text-mist text-sm leading-relaxed flex-grow mb-4 line-clamp-3">
          {tool.description}
        </p>

        {/* Rating */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 mb-4">
          <Star size={12} className="text-gold fill-gold" />
          <span className="text-sm font-mono text-paper">{tool.rating?.toFixed(1) || "N/A"}</span>
        </div>

        {/* Footer: pricing + category */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2 pt-3 border-t border-paper/5">
          <span className={`inline-block text-[10px] font-mono uppercase tracking-wider px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${colorClass}`}>
            {formatPricing(tool.pricing)}
          </span>
          <span className="font-mono text-[10px] text-mist/40 uppercase tracking-wider truncate">
            {tool.category.replace(/_/g, " ")}
          </span>
        </div>

        {/* Tags */}
        {tool.tags && tool.tags.length > 0 && (
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1 mt-3">
            {tool.tags.slice(0, 3).map((tag) => (
              <span key={tag} className="text-[9px] font-mono px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-gold/5 text-mist/50">
                {tag}
              </span>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </Link>
  );
}

import ToolCard from "./ToolCard";

interface Tool {
  name: string;
  slug: string;
  description: string;
  website: string;
  category: string;
  pricing: string;
  company: string;
  tags: string[];
}

export default function ToolGrid({ tools }: { tools: Tool[] }) {
  if (!tools || tools.length === 0) {
    return (
      <div className="flex items-center justify-center py-20">
        <p className="text-mist/60 font-mono text-sm">No tools found.</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
      {tools.map((tool) => (
        <ToolCard key={tool.slug} tool={tool} />
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}


╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ FILE: ./components/WorkflowCard.tsx
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

import Link from "next/link";
import { ArrowRight, Workflow as WorkflowIcon, ChevronRight } from "lucide-react";

interface WorkflowStep {
  step_order: number;
  tool_slug: string;
  description: string;
}

interface Workflow {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  slug: string;
  description: string;
  use_case: string;
  steps: WorkflowStep[];
}

export default function WorkflowCard({ workflow }: { workflow: Workflow }) {
  return (
    <Link href={`/workflows/${workflow.slug}`} className="group block">
      <div className="bg-surface border border-gold/5 rounded-sm p-6 transition-all duration-300 hover:border-gold/30 hover:-translate-y-1">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-4">
          <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-teal/10 rounded-sm flex items-center justify-center">
            <WorkflowIcon size={18} className="text-teal-light" />
          </div>
          <span className="text-[10px] font-mono uppercase tracking-wider px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-gold/10 text-gold">
            {workflow.use_case}
          </span>
        </div>

        {/* Name */}
        <h3 className="font-display text-xl text-paper mb-2 group-hover:text-gold transition-colors">
          {workflow.name}
        </h3>
        <p className="text-mist text-sm mb-4 line-clamp-2">{workflow.description}</p>

        {/* Steps preview */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1 flex-wrap">
          {workflow.steps.map((step, i) => (
            <span key={step.step_order} className="flex items-center gap-1">
              <span className="text-xs font-mono px-2 py-0.5 bg-paper/5 border border-paper/10 rounded-sm text-mist">
                {step.tool_slug.replace(/-/g, " ")}
              </span>
              {i < workflow.steps.length - 1 && (
                <ChevronRight size={10} className="text-gold/40" />
              )}
            </span>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Footer */}
        <div className="mt-4 pt-3 border-t border-paper/5 flex items-center justify-between">
          <span className="font-mono text-xs text-mist/50">{workflow.steps.length} steps</span>
          <ArrowRight size={14} className="text-mist/0 group-hover:text-gold transition-all duration-300" />
        </div>
      </div>
    </Link>
  );
}
